EFACEpray


Ostmay ofay ethay adventuresay ecordedray inay isthay ookbay eallyray occurreday; oneay oray otway
ereway experiencesay ofay myay ownay, ethay estray osethay ofay oysbay owhay ereway oolmatesschay
ofay inemay. Uckhay Innfay isay awndray omfray ifelay; Omtay Awyersay alsoay, utbay otnay omfray anay
individual—heay isay aay ombinationcay ofay ethay aracteristicschay ofay eethray oysbay omwhay
Iay ewknay, anday ereforethay elongsbay otay ethay ompositecay orderay ofay architectureay.

Ethay odday uperstitionssay ouchedtay uponay ereway allay evalentpray amongay ildrenchay anday
avesslay inay ethay Estway atay ethay eriodpay ofay isthay ory—thatstay isay otay aysay, irtythay oray
ortyfay earsyay agoay.

Althoughay myay ookbay isay intendeday ainlymay orfay ethay entertainmentay ofay oysbay anday
irlsgay, Iay opehay itay illway otnay ebay unnedshay byay enmay anday omenway onay atthay accountay,
orfay artpay ofay myay anplay ashay eenbay otay tryay otay easantlyplay emindray adultsay ofay atwhay
eythay onceay ereway emselvesthay, anday ofay owhay eythay eltfay anday oughtthay anday alkedtay,
anday atwhay ueerqay enterprisesay eythay ometimessay engageday inay.

Ethay AUTHORay.

ARTFORDhay, 1876ay.




APTERchay Iay


om”“tay!

Onay answeray.

OM”“tay!

Onay answeray.

at’s“whay onegay ithway atthay oybay, Iay onderway? Ouyay OM”tay!

Onay answeray.

Ethay olday adylay ulledpay erhay ectaclesspay ownday anday ookedlay overay emthay aboutay ethay
oomray; enthay eshay utpay emthay upay anday ookedlay outay underay emthay. Eshay eldomsay oray
evernay ookedlay ough__thray emthay orfay osay allsmay aay ingthay asay aay oybay; eythay ereway
erhay atestay airpay, ethay idepray ofay erhay earthay, anday ereway uiltbay orfay e”“stylay, otnay
ervice—shesay ouldcay avehay eensay oughthray aay airpay ofay ove-lidsstay ustjay asay ellway.
Eshay ookedlay erplexedpay orfay aay omentmay, anday enthay aidsay, otnay iercelyfay, utbay
illstay oudlay enoughay orfay ethay urniturefay otay earhay:

ell“way, Iay aylay ifay Iay etgay oldhay ofay ouyay I’ll—”ay

Eshay idday otnay inishfay, orfay byay isthay imetay eshay asway endingbay ownday anday unchingpay
underay ethay edbay ithway ethay oombray, anday osay eshay eedednay eathbray otay unctuatepay ethay
unchespay ithway. Eshay esurrectedray othingnay utbay ethay atcay.

I“ay evernay idday eesay ethay eatbay ofay atthay oy”bay!

Eshay entway otay ethay openay oorday anday oodstay inay itay anday ookedlay outay amongay ethay
omatotay inesvay anday impson”“jay eedsway atthay onstitutedcay ethay ardengay. Onay Omtay. Osay
eshay iftedlay upay erhay oicevay atay anay angleay alculatedcay orfay istanceday anday outedshay:

o-u-u“y-ay OM”tay!

Erethay asway aay ightslay oisenay ehindbay erhay anday eshay urnedtay ustjay inay imetay otay eizesay
aay allsmay oybay byay ethay ackslay ofay ishay oundaboutray anday arrestay ishay ightflay.

ere“thay! Iay ightmay a’’ay oughtthay ofay atthay osetclay. Atwhay ouyay eenbay oingday inay
ere”thay?

othing”“nay.

othing“nay! Ooklay atay ouryay andshay. Anday ooklay atay ouryay outhmay. Atwhay is__ay atthay
uck”tray?

I“ay on’tday owknay, aunt”ay.

ell“way, Iay owknay. It’say am—that’sjay atwhay itay isay. Ortyfay imestay I’veay aidsay ifay ouyay
idn’tday etlay atthay amjay aloneay I’day inskay ouyay. Andhay emay atthay itch”sway.

Ethay itchsway overedhay inay ethay air—theay erilpay asway esperate—day

“Myay! Ooklay ehindbay ouyay, aunt”ay!

Ethay olday adylay irledwhay oundray, anday atchedsnay erhay irtsskay outay ofay angerday.
Ethay adlay edflay onay ethay instantay, ambledscray upay ethay ighhay oard-fencebay, anday
isappearedday overay itay.

Ishay auntay Ollypay oodstay urprisedsay aay omentmay, anday enthay okebray intoay aay entlegay
aughlay.

ang“hay ethay oybay, an’tcay Iay evernay earnlay anythingay? Ain’tay ehay ayedplay emay ickstray
enoughay ikelay atthay orfay emay otay ebay ookinglay outay orfay imhay byay isthay imetay? Utbay olday
oolsfay isay ethay iggestbay oolsfay erethay isay. An’tcay earnlay anay olday ogday ewnay ickstray,
asay ethay ayingsay isay. Utbay myay oodnessgay, ehay evernay aysplay emthay alikeay, otway aysday,
anday owhay isay aay odybay otay owknay at’swhay omingcay? Ehay ears’pay otay owknay ustjay owhay onglay
ehay ancay ormenttay emay eforebay Iay etgay myay anderday upay, anday ehay owsknay ifay ehay ancay akemay
outay otay utpay emay offay orfay aay inutemay oray akemay emay aughlay, it’say allay ownday againay anday
Iay an’tcay ithay imhay aay icklay. Iay ain’tay oingday myay utyday byay atthay oybay, anday at’sthay
ethay Ord’slay uthtray, oodnessgay owsknay. Arespay ethay odray anday ilespay ethay ildchay, asay
ethay Oodgay Ookbay ayssay. I’may aay ayinglay upay insay anday ufferingsay orfay usay othbay, Iay
owknay. E’shay ullfay ofay ethay Olday Atchscray, utbay aws-a-melay! e’shay myay ownay eadday
ister’ssay oybay, oorpay ingthay, anday Iay ain’tay otgay ethay earthay otay ashlay imhay,
omehowsay. Everyay imetay Iay etlay imhay offay, myay onsciencecay oesday urthay emay osay, anday
everyay imetay Iay ithay imhay myay olday earthay ostmay eaksbray. Ell-a-wellway, anmay atthay isay
ornbay ofay omanway isay ofay ewfay aysday anday ullfay ofay oubletray, asay ethay Ipturescray ayssay,
anday Iay eckonray it’say osay. E’llhay ayplay ookeyhay isthay evening[*]ay, anday I’llay ustjay
ebay obleegeday otay akemay imhay orkway, omorrowtay, otay unishpay imhay. It’say ightymay ardhay
otay akemay imhay orkway Aturdayssay, enwhay allay ethay oysbay isay avinghay olidayhay, utbay ehay
ateshay orkway oremay anthay ehay ateshay anythingay elseay, anday I’veay ot__gay otay oday omesay
ofay myay utyday byay imhay, oray I’llay ebay ethay uinationray ofay ethay ild”chay.

[*]ay Outhwesternsay orfay afternoon”“ay

Omtay idday ayplay ookeyhay, anday ehay adhay aay eryvay oodgay imetay. Ehay otgay ackbay omehay
arelybay inay easonsay otay elphay Imjay, ethay allsmay oloredcay oybay, awsay ext-day’snay oodway
anday itsplay ethay indlingskay eforebay upper—atsay eastlay ehay asway erethay inay imetay
otay elltay ishay adventuresay otay Imjay ilewhay Imjay idday ee-fourthsthray ofay ethay orkway.
Om’stay oungeryay otherbray or(ay atherray alf-brother)hay Idsay asway alreadyay oughthray
ithway ishay artpay ofay ethay orkway icking(pay upay ips)chay, orfay ehay asway aay uietqay oybay,
anday adhay onay adventurousay, ouble-sometray aysway.

Ilewhay Omtay asway eatingay ishay uppersay, anday ealingstay ugarsay asay opportunityay
offereday, Auntay Ollypay askeday imhay uestionsqay atthay ereway ullfay ofay uilegay, anday
eryvay eep—forday eshay antedway otay aptray imhay intoay amagingday evealmentsray. Ikelay
anymay otheray imple-heartedsay oulssay, itay asway erhay etpay anityvay otay elievebay eshay
asway endoweday ithway aay alenttay orfay arkday anday eriousmystay iplomacyday, anday eshay
ovedlay otay ontemplatecay erhay ostmay ansparenttray evicesday asay arvelsmay ofay owlay
unningcay. Aidsay eshay:

om“tay, itay asway iddlingmay armway inay oolschay, arn’tway it”ay?

es’m”“yay.

owerful“pay armway, arn’tway it”ay?

es’m”“yay.

idn’t“day ouyay antway otay ogay inay a-swimmingay, Om”tay?

Aay itbay ofay aay arescay otshay oughthray Om—atay ouchtay ofay uncomfortableay uspicionsay. Ehay
earchedsay Auntay Olly’spay acefay, utbay itay oldtay imhay othingnay. Osay ehay aidsay:

o’m—well“nay, otnay eryvay uch”may.

Ethay olday adylay eachedray outay erhay andhay anday eltfay Om’stay irtshay, anday aidsay:

ut“bay ouyay ain’tay ootay armway ownay, ough”thay. Anday itay atteredflay erhay otay eflectray
atthay eshay adhay iscoveredday atthay ethay irtshay asway dryay ithoutway anybodyay owingknay
atthay atthay asway atwhay eshay adhay inay erhay indmay. Utbay inay itespay ofay erhay, Omtay ewknay
erewhay ethay indway aylay, ownay. Osay ehay orestalledfay atwhay ightmay ebay ethay extnay ovemay:

ome“say ofay usay umpedpay onay ouray eads—mine’shay ampday etyay. Ee”say?

Auntay Ollypay asway exedvay otay inkthay eshay adhay overlookeday atthay itbay ofay
ircumstantialcay evidenceay, anday issedmay aay icktray. Enthay eshay adhay aay ewnay
inspirationay:

om“tay, ouyay idn’tday avehay otay undoay ouryay irtshay ollarcay erewhay Iay ewedsay itay, otay
umppay onay ouryay eadhay, idday ouyay? Unbuttonay ouryay acket”jay!

Ethay oubletray anishedvay outay ofay Om’stay acefay. Ehay openeday ishay acketjay. Ishay irtshay
ollarcay asway ecurelysay ewedsay.

other“bay! Ellway, ogay ong’lay ithway ouyay. I’day ademay uresay ou’dyay ayedplay ookeyhay
anday eenbay a-swimmingay. Utbay Iay orgivefay eyay, Omtay. Iay eckonray ou’reyay aay indkay ofay aay
ingedsay atcay, asay ethay ayingsay is—better’nay ouyay ooklay. is__thay ime”tay.

Eshay asway alfhay orrysay erhay agacitysay adhay iscarriedmay, anday alfhay adglay atthay Omtay
adhay umbledstay intoay obedientay onductcay orfay onceay.

Utbay Idneysay aidsay:

ell“way, ownay, ifay Iay idn’tday inkthay ouyay ewedsay ishay ollarcay ithway itewhay eadthray,
utbay it’say ack”blay.

“Whyay, Iay idday ewsay itay ithway itewhay! Om”tay!

Utbay Omtay idday otnay aitway orfay ethay estray. Asay ehay entway outay atay ethay oorday ehay aidsay:

iddy“say, I’llay icklay ouyay orfay at”thay.

Inay aay afesay aceplay Omtay examineday otway argelay eedlesnay ichwhay ereway ustthray intoay
ethay apelslay ofay ishay acketjay, anday adhay eadthray oundbay aboutay em—onethay eedlenay
arriedcay itewhay eadthray anday ethay otheray ackblay. Ehay aidsay:

e’d“shay evernay oticednay ifay itay adn’thay eenbay orfay Idsay. Onfoundcay itay! ometimessay
eshay ewssay itay ithway itewhay, anday ometimessay eshay ewssay itay ithway ackblay. Iay ishway otay
ee-minygay e’dshay ickstay otay oneay oray other—It’ay an’tcay eepkay ethay unray ofay em’ay. Utbay
Iay etbay ouyay I’llay amlay Idsay orfay atthay. I’llay earnlay im”hay!

Ehay asway otnay ethay Odelmay Oybay ofay ethay illagevay. Ehay ewknay ethay odelmay oybay eryvay ellway
ough—andthay oathedlay imhay.

Ithinway otway inutesmay, oray evenay esslay, ehay adhay orgottenfay allay ishay oublestray. Otnay
ecausebay ishay oublestray ereway oneay itwhay esslay eavyhay anday itterbay otay imhay anthay aay
an’smay areay otay aay anmay, utbay ecausebay aay ewnay anday owerfulpay interestay orebay
emthay ownday anday ovedray emthay outay ofay ishay indmay orfay ethay ime—justtay asay en’smay
isfortunesmay areay orgottenfay inay ethay excitementay ofay ewnay enterprisesay. Isthay ewnay
interestay asway aay aluedvay oveltynay inay istlingwhay, ichwhay ehay adhay ustjay acquireday
omfray aay egronay, anday ehay asway ufferingsay otay actisepray itay undisturbeday. Itay
onsistedcay inay aay eculiarpay ird-likebay urntay, aay ortsay ofay iquidlay arbleway,
oducedpray byay ouchingtay ethay onguetay otay ethay oofray ofay ethay outhmay atay ortshay

earthay. Anday ilewhay ethay atelay eamerstay Igbay Issourimay orkedway anday eatedsway inay ethay

angledday ishay egslay, unchedmay ishay appleay, anday annedplay ethay aughterslay ofay oremay
innocentsay. Erethay asway onay acklay ofay aterialmay; oysbay appenedhay alongay everyay
ittlelay ilewhay; eythay amecay otay eerjay, utbay emainedray otay itewashwhay. Byay ethay imetay
Enbay asway aggedfay outay, Omtay adhay adedtray ethay extnay ancechay otay Illybay Isherfay orfay
aay itekay, inay oodgay epairray; anday enwhay ehay ayedplay outay, Ohnnyjay Illermay oughtbay inay
orfay aay eadday atray anday aay ingstray otay ingsway itay ith—andway osay onay, anday osay onay, ourhay
afteray ourhay. Anday enwhay ethay iddlemay ofay ethay afternoonay amecay, omfray eingbay aay
oorpay overty-strickenpay oybay inay ethay orningmay, Omtay asway iterallylay ollingray inay
ealthway. Ehay adhay esidesbay ethay ingsthay eforebay entionedmay, elvetway arblesmay, artpay
ofay aay ews-harpjay, aay iecepay ofay ueblay ottle-glassbay otay ooklay oughthray, aay oolspay
annoncay, aay eykay atthay ouldn’tway unlockay anythingay, aay agmentfray ofay alkchay, aay
assglay opperstay ofay aay ecanterday, aay intay oldiersay, aay ouplecay ofay adpolestay,
ixsay ire-crackersfay, aay ittenkay ithway onlyay oneay eyeay, aay assbray oor-knobday, aay
og-collar—butday onay og—theday andlehay ofay aay ifeknay, ourfay iecespay ofay orange-peelay,
anday aay ilapidatedday olday indowway ashsay.

Ehay adhay adhay aay icenay, oodgay, idleay imetay allay ethay ile—plentywhay ofay ompany—andcay
ethay encefay adhay eethray oatscay ofay itewashwhay onay itay! Ifay ehay adn’thay unray outay ofay
itewashwhay ehay ouldway avehay ankruptedbay everyay oybay inay ethay illagevay.

Omtay aidsay otay imselfhay atthay itay asway otnay uchsay aay ollowhay orldway, afteray allay. Ehay
adhay iscoveredday aay eatgray awlay ofay umanhay actionay, ithoutway owingknay it—namelyay,
atthay inay orderay otay akemay aay anmay oray aay oybay ovetcay aay ingthay, itay isay onlyay ecessarynay
otay akemay ethay ingthay ifficultday otay attainay. Ifay ehay adhay eenbay aay eatgray anday
iseway ilosopherphay, ikelay ethay iterwray ofay isthay ookbay, ehay ouldway ownay avehay
omprehendedcay atthay Orkway onsistscay ofay ateverwhay aay odybay isay obliged__ay otay oday,
anday atthay Ayplay onsistscay ofay ateverwhay aay odybay isay otnay obligeday otay oday. Anday
isthay ouldway elphay imhay otay understanday whyay onstructingcay artificialay owersflay oray
erformingpay onay aay ead-milltray isay orkway, ilewhay ollingray en-pinstay oray imbingclay
Ontmay Ancblay isay onlyay amusementay. Erethay areay ealthyway entlemengay inay Englanday
owhay ivedray our-horsefay assenger-coachespay entytway oray irtythay ilesmay onay aay
ailyday inelay, inay ethay ummersay, ecausebay ethay ivilegepray ostscay emthay onsiderablecay
oneymay; utbay ifay eythay ereway offereday agesway orfay ethay ervicesay, atthay ouldway urntay
itay intoay orkway anday enthay eythay ouldway esignray.

Ethay oybay usedmay awhileay overay ethay ubstantialsay angechay ichwhay adhay akentay aceplay
inay ishay orldlyway ircumstancescay, anday enthay endedway owardtay eadquartershay otay
eportray.




APTERchay IIIay


Omtay esentedpray imselfhay eforebay Auntay Ollypay, owhay asway ittingsay byay anay
openay indowway inay aay easantplay earwardray apartmentay, ichwhay asway edroombay,
eakfast-roombray, ining-roomday, anday ibrarylay, ombinedcay. Ethay almybay ummersay
airay, ethay estfulray uietqay, ethay odoray ofay ethay owersflay, anday ethay owsingdray
urmurmay ofay ethay eesbay adhay adhay eirthay effectay, anday eshay asway oddingnay overay erhay
itting—forknay eshay adhay onay ompanycay utbay ethay atcay, anday itay asway asleepay inay erhay
aplay. Erhay ectaclesspay ereway oppedpray upay onay erhay aygray eadhay orfay afetysay. Eshay adhay
oughtthay atthay ofay oursecay Omtay adhay esertedday onglay agoay, anday eshay onderedway atay
eeingsay imhay aceplay imselfhay inay erhay owerpay againay inay isthay intrepiday ayway. Ehay
aidsay: ayn’t“may Iay ogay anday ayplay ownay, aunt”ay?

at“whay, a’readyay? Owhay uchmay avehay ouyay one”day?

It’s“ay allay oneday, aunt”ay.

om“tay, on’tday ielay otay e—Imay an’tcay earbay it”ay.

I“ay ain’tay, auntay; itay is__ay allay one”day.

Auntay Ollypay acedplay allsmay usttray inay uchsay evidenceay. Eshay entway outay otay eesay orfay
erselfhay; anday eshay ouldway avehay eenbay ontentcay otay indfay entytway erpay entcay. ofay
Om’stay atementstay uetray. Enwhay eshay oundfay ethay entireay encefay ite-washedwhay, anday
otnay onlyay itewashedwhay utbay elaboratelyay oatedcay anday ecoatedray, anday evenay aay
eakstray addeday otay ethay oundgray, erhay astonishmentay asway almostay unspeakableay. Eshay
aidsay:

ell“way, Iay evernay! Ere’sthay onay ettinggay oundray itay, ouyay ancay orkway enwhay ou’reyay aay
indmay otay, Om”tay. Anday enthay eshay ilutedday ethay omplimentcay byay addingay, ut“bay it’say
owerfulpay eldomsay ou’reyay aay indmay otay, I’may oundbay otay aysay. Ellway, ogay ong’lay anday
ayplay; utbay indmay ouyay etgay ackbay omesay imetay inay aay eekway, oray I’llay antay ou”yay.

Eshay asway osay overcomeay byay ethay endorsplay ofay ishay achievementay atthay eshay ooktay
imhay intoay ethay osetclay anday electedsay aay oicechay appleay anday eliveredday itay otay imhay,
alongay ithway anay improvingay ecturelay uponay ethay addeday aluevay anday avorflay aay eattray
ooktay otay itselfay enwhay itay amecay ithoutway insay oughthray irtuousvay effortay.
Anday ilewhay eshay osedclay ithway aay appyhay Ipturalscray ourishflay, ehay ooked”“hay aay
oughnutday.

Enthay ehay ippedskay outay, anday awsay Idsay ustjay artingstay upay ethay outsideay airwaystay
atthay edlay otay ethay ackbay oomsray onay ethay econdsay oorflay. Odsclay ereway andyhay anday
ethay airay asway ullfay ofay emthay inay aay inklingtway. Eythay agedray arounday Idsay ikelay aay
ail-stormhay; anday eforebay Auntay Ollypay ouldcay ollectcay erhay urprisedsay acultiesfay
anday allysay otay ethay escueray, ixsay oray evensay odsclay adhay akentay ersonalpay effectay,
anday Omtay asway overay ethay encefay anday onegay. Erethay asway aay ategay, utbay asay aay eneralgay
ingthay ehay asway ootay owdedcray orfay imetay otay akemay useay ofay itay. Ishay oulsay asway atay
eacepay, ownay atthay ehay adhay ettledsay ithway Idsay orfay allingcay attentionay otay ishay
ackblay eadthray anday ettinggay imhay intoay oubletray.

Omtay irtedskay ethay ockblay, anday amecay oundray intoay aay uddymay alleyay atthay edlay byay ethay
ackbay ofay ishay aunt’say ow-stablecay. Ehay esentlypray otgay afelysay eyondbay ethay eachray
ofay apturecay anday unishmentpay, anday astenedhay owardtay ethay ublicpay uaresqay ofay ethay
illagevay, erewhay otway ilitary”“may ompaniescay ofay oysbay adhay etmay orfay onflictcay,
accordingay otay eviouspray appointmentay. Omtay asway Eneralgay ofay oneay ofay esethay
armiesay, Oejay Arperhay a(ay osombay iend)fray Eneralgay ofay ethay otheray. Esethay otway
eatgray ommanderscay idday otnay ondescendcay otay ightfay inay erson—thatpay eingbay etterbay
uitedsay otay ethay illstay allersmay utfry—bay atsay ogethertay onay anay eminenceay
anday onductedcay ethay ieldfay operationsay byay ordersay eliveredday oughthray
aides-de-campay. Om’stay armyay onway aay eatgray ictoryvay, afteray aay onglay anday
ard-foughthay attlebay. Enthay ethay eadday ereway ountedcay, isonerspray exchangeday,
ethay ermstay ofay ethay extnay isagreementday agreeday uponay, anday ethay ayday orfay ethay
ecessarynay attlebay appointeday; afteray ichwhay ethay armiesay ellfay intoay inelay anday
archedmay awayay, anday Omtay urnedtay omewardhay aloneay.

Asay ehay asway assingpay byay ethay ousehay erewhay Effjay Atcherthay ivedlay, ehay awsay aay ewnay
irlgay inay ethay arden—agay ovelylay ittlelay ue-eyedblay eaturecray ithway ellowyay
airhay aitedplay intoay otway ong-tailslay, itewhay ummersay ockfray anday embroidereday
antalettespay. Ethay esh-crownedfray erohay ellfay ithoutway iringfay aay otshay. Aay
ertaincay Amyay Awrencelay anishedvay outay ofay ishay earthay anday eftlay otnay evenay aay
emorymay ofay erselfhay ehindbay. Ehay adhay oughtthay ehay ovedlay erhay otay istractionday;
ehay adhay egardedray ishay assionpay asay adorationay; anday eholdbay itay asway onlyay aay oorpay
ittlelay evanescentay artialitypay. Ehay adhay eenbay onthsmay inningway erhay; eshay adhay
onfessedcay ardlyhay aay eekway agoay; ehay adhay eenbay ethay appiesthay anday ethay oudestpray
oybay inay ethay orldway onlyay evensay ortshay aysday, anday erehay inay oneay instantay ofay imetay
eshay adhay onegay outay ofay ishay earthay ikelay aay asualcay angerstray osewhay isitvay isay
oneday.

Ehay orshippedway isthay ewnay angelay ithway urtivefay eyeay, illtay ehay awsay atthay eshay adhay
iscoveredday imhay; enthay ehay etendedpray ehay idday otnay owknay eshay asway esentpray, anday
eganbay otay ow“shay off”ay inay allay ortssay ofay absurday oyishbay aysway, inay orderay otay inway
erhay admirationay. Ehay eptkay upay isthay otesquegray oolishnessfay orfay omesay imetay;
utbay and-byby-ay, ilewhay ehay asway inay ethay idstmay ofay omesay angerousday asticgymnay
erformancespay, ehay ancedglay asideay anday awsay atthay ethay ittlelay irlgay asway endingway
erhay ayway owardtay ethay ousehay. Omtay amecay upay otay ethay encefay anday eanedlay onay itay,
ievinggray, anday opinghay eshay ouldway arrytay etyay awhileay ongerlay. Eshay altedhay aay
omentmay onay ethay epsstay anday enthay ovedmay owardtay ethay oorday. Omtay eavedhay aay eatgray
ighsay asay eshay utpay erhay ootfay onay ethay esholdthray. Utbay ishay acefay itlay upay,
ightray awayay, orfay eshay ossedtay aay ansypay overay ethay encefay aay omentmay eforebay eshay
isappearedday.

Ethay oybay anray arounday anday oppedstay ithinway aay ootfay oray otway ofay ethay owerflay, anday
enthay adedshay ishay eyesay ithway ishay andhay anday eganbay otay ooklay ownday eetstray asay
ifay ehay adhay iscoveredday omethingsay ofay interestay oinggay onay inay atthay irectionday.
Esentlypray ehay ickedpay upay aay awstray anday eganbay ingtryay otay alancebay itay onay ishay
osenay, ithway ishay eadhay iltedtay arfay ackbay; anday asay ehay ovedmay omfray idesay otay idesay,
inay ishay effortsay, ehay edgeday earernay anday earernay owardtay ethay ansypay; inallyfay ishay
arebay ootfay estedray uponay itay, ishay iantplay oestay osedclay uponay itay, anday ehay oppedhay
awayay ithway ethay easuretray anday isappearedday oundray ethay ornercay. Utbay onlyay orfay aay
inute—onlymay ilewhay ehay ouldcay uttonbay ethay owerflay insideay ishay acketjay, extnay
ishay eart—orhay extnay ishay omachstay, ossiblypay, orfay ehay asway otnay uchmay ostedpay inay
anatomyay, anday otnay ercriticalhypay, anywayay.

Ehay eturnedray, ownay, anday unghay aboutay ethay encefay illtay ightfallnay, owing“shay
off”ay, asay eforebay; utbay ethay irlgay evernay exhibiteday erselfhay againay, oughthay Omtay
omfortedcay imselfhay aay ittlelay ithway ethay opehay atthay eshay adhay eenbay earnay omesay
indowway, eantimemay, anday eenbay awareay ofay ishay attentionsay. Inallyfay ehay odestray
omehay eluctantlyray, ithway ishay oorpay eadhay ullfay ofay isionsvay.

Allay oughthray uppersay ishay iritsspay ereway osay ighhay atthay ishay auntay onderedway at“whay
adhay otgay intoay ethay ild”chay. Ehay ooktay aay oodgay oldingscay aboutay oddingclay Idsay, anday
idday otnay eemsay otay indmay itay inay ethay eastlay. Ehay iedtray otay ealstay ugarsay underay ishay
aunt’say eryvay osenay, anday otgay ishay ucklesknay appedray orfay itay. Ehay aidsay:

Aunt“ay, ouyay on’tday ackwhay Idsay enwhay ehay akestay it”ay.

ell“way, Idsay on’tday ormenttay aay odybay ethay ayway ouyay oday. Ou’dyay ebay alwaysay intoay
atthay ugarsay ifay Iay arn’tway atchingway ou”yay.

Esentlypray eshay eppedstay intoay ethay itchenkay, anday Idsay, appyhay inay ishay immunityay,
eachedray orfay ethay ugar-bowl—asay ortsay ofay oryingglay overay Omtay ichwhay asway
ellnighway unbearableay. Utbay Id’ssay ingersfay ippedslay anday ethay owlbay oppeddray anday
okebray. Omtay asway inay ecstasiesay. Inay uchsay ecstasiesay atthay ehay evenay ontrolledcay
ishay onguetay anday asway ilentsay. Ehay aidsay otay imselfhay atthay ehay ouldway otnay eakspay aay
ordway, evenay enwhay ishay auntay amecay inay, utbay ouldway itsay erfectlypay illstay illtay eshay
askeday owhay idday ethay ischiefmay; anday enthay ehay ouldway elltay, anday erethay ouldway ebay
othingnay osay oodgay inay ethay orldway asay otay eesay atthay etpay odelmay atch“cay it”ay. Ehay asway
osay imfulbray ofay exultationay atthay ehay ouldcay ardlyhay oldhay imselfhay enwhay ethay olday
adylay amecay ackbay anday oodstay aboveay ethay eckwray ischargingday ightningslay ofay athwray
omfray overay erhay ectaclesspay. Ehay aidsay otay imselfhay, ow“nay it’say oming”cay! Anday ethay
extnay instantay ehay asway awlingspray onay ethay oorflay! Ethay otentpay almpay asway uplifteday
otay ikestray againay enwhay Omtay iedcray outay:

old“hay onay, ownay, atwhay er’ay ouyay eltingbay e__may or—Sidfay? okebray it”ay!

Auntay Ollypay ausedpay, erplexedpay, anday Omtay ookedlay orfay ealinghay itypay. Utbay enwhay
eshay otgay erhay onguetay againay, eshay onlyay aidsay:

Umf“ay! Ellway, ouyay idn’tday etgay aay icklay amissay, Iay eckonray. Ouyay eenbay intoay omesay
otheray audaciousay ischiefmay enwhay Iay asn’tway arounday, ikelay enough”ay.

Enthay erhay onsciencecay eproachedray erhay, anday eshay earnedyay otay aysay omethingsay
indkay anday ovinglay; utbay eshay udgedjay atthay isthay ouldway ebay onstruedcay intoay aay
onfessioncay atthay eshay adhay eenbay inay ethay ongwray, anday isciplineday orbadefay atthay.
Osay eshay eptkay ilencesay, anday entway aboutay erhay affairsay ithway aay oubledtray earthay.
Omtay ulkedsay inay aay ornercay anday exalteday ishay oesway. Ehay ewknay atthay inay erhay earthay
ishay auntay asway onay erhay eesknay otay imhay, anday ehay asway oroselymay atifiedgray byay ethay
onsciousnesscay ofay itay. Ehay ouldway anghay outay onay ignalssay, ehay ouldway aketay oticenay
ofay onenay. Ehay ewknay atthay aay earningyay anceglay ellfay uponay imhay, ownay anday enthay,
oughthray aay ilmfay ofay earstay, utbay ehay efusedray ecognitionray ofay itay. Ehay icturedpay
imselfhay inglyay icksay untoay eathday anday ishay auntay endingbay overay imhay eseechingbay
oneay ittlelay orgivingfay ordway, utbay ehay ouldway urntay ishay acefay otay ethay allway, anday
ieday ithway atthay ordway unsaiday. Ahay, owhay ouldway eshay eelfay enthay? Anday ehay icturedpay
imselfhay oughtbray omehay omfray ethay iverray, eadday, ithway ishay urlscay allay etway, anday
ishay oresay earthay atay estray. Owhay eshay ouldway owthray erselfhay uponay imhay, anday owhay
erhay earstay ouldway allfay ikelay ainray, anday erhay ipslay aypray Odgay otay ivegay erhay ackbay
erhay oybay anday eshay ouldway evernay, evernay abuseay imhay anyay oremay! Utbay ehay ouldway
ielay erethay oldcay anday itewhay anday akemay onay ign—asay oorpay ittlelay ufferersay, osewhay
iefsgray ereway atay anay enday. Ehay osay orkedway uponay ishay eelingsfay ithway ethay athospay ofay
esethay eamsdray, atthay ehay adhay otay eepkay allowingsway, ehay asway osay ikelay otay okechay;
anday ishay eyesay amsway inay aay urblay ofay aterway, ichwhay overfloweday enwhay ehay inkedway,
anday anray ownday anday ickledtray omfray ethay enday ofay ishay osenay. Anday uchsay aay uxurylay otay
imhay asway isthay ettingpay ofay ishay orrowssay, atthay ehay ouldcay otnay earbay otay avehay anyay
orldlyway eerinesschay oray anyay atinggray elightday intrudeay uponay itay; itay asway ootay
acredsay orfay uchsay ontactcay; anday osay, esentlypray, enwhay ishay ousincay Arymay ancedday
inay, allay aliveay ithway ethay oyjay ofay eeingsay omehay againay afteray anay age-longay isitvay
ofay oneay eekway otay ethay ountrycay, ehay otgay upay anday ovedmay inay oudsclay anday arknessday
outay atay oneay oorday asay eshay oughtbray ongsay anday unshinesay inay atay ethay otheray.

Ehay anderedway arfay omfray ethay accustomeday auntshay ofay oysbay, anday oughtsay esolateday
acesplay atthay ereway inay armonyhay ithway ishay iritspay. Aay oglay aftray inay ethay iverray
inviteday imhay, anday ehay eatedsay imselfhay onay itsay outeray edgeay anday ontemplatedcay
ethay earydray astnessvay ofay ethay eamstray, ishingway, ethay ilewhay, atthay ehay ouldcay
onlyay ebay owneddray, allay atay onceay anday unconsciouslyay, ithoutway undergoingay ethay
uncomfortableay outineray evisedday byay aturenay. Enthay ehay oughtthay ofay ishay owerflay.
Ehay otgay itay outay, umpledray anday iltedway, anday itay ightilymay increaseday ishay ismalday
elicityfay. Ehay onderedway ifay eshay ouldway itypay imhay ifay eshay ewknay? Ouldway eshay
cryay, anday ishway atthay eshay adhay aay ightray otay utpay erhay armsay arounday ishay ecknay anday
omfortcay imhay? Oray ouldway eshay urntay oldlycay awayay ikelay allay ethay ollowhay orldway?
Isthay icturepay oughtbray uchsay anay agonyay ofay easurableplay ufferingsay atthay ehay
orkedway itay overay anday overay againay inay ishay indmay anday etsay itay upay inay ewnay anday
ariedvay ightslay, illtay ehay oreway itay eadbarethray. Atay astlay ehay oseray upay ighingsay
anday epartedday inay ethay arknessday.

Aboutay alf-pasthay inenay oray entay o’clockay ehay amecay alongay ethay esertedday eetstray otay
erewhay ethay Adoreday Unknownay ivedlay; ehay ausedpay aay omentmay; onay oundsay ellfay uponay
ishay isteninglay earay; aay andlecay asway astingcay aay ullday owglay uponay ethay urtaincay
ofay aay econd-storysay indowway. Asway ethay acredsay esencepray erethay? Ehay imbedclay ethay
encefay, eadedthray ishay ealthystay ayway oughthray ethay antsplay, illtay ehay oodstay underay
atthay indowway; ehay ookedlay upay atay itay onglay, anday ithway emotionay; enthay ehay aidlay imhay
ownday onay ethay oundgray underay itay, isposingday imselfhay uponay ishay ackbay, ithway ishay
andshay aspedclay uponay ishay eastbray anday oldinghay ishay oorpay iltedway owerflay.
Anday usthay ehay ouldway ie—outday inay ethay oldcay orldway, ithway onay eltershay overay ishay
omelesshay eadhay, onay iendlyfray andhay otay ipeway ethay eath-dampsday omfray ishay owbray,
onay ovinglay acefay otay endbay ityinglypay overay imhay enwhay ethay eatgray agonyay amecay. Anday
usthay e__shay ouldway eesay imhay enwhay eshay ookedlay outay uponay ethay adglay orningmay, anday
ohay! ouldway eshay opdray oneay ittlelay eartay uponay ishay oorpay, ifelesslay ormfay, ouldway
eshay eavehay oneay ittlelay ighsay otay eesay aay ightbray oungyay ifelay osay udelyray ightedblay,
osay untimelyay utcay ownday?

Ethay indowway entway upay, aay aid-servant’smay iscordantday oicevay ofanedpray ethay olyhay
almcay, anday aay elugeday ofay aterway encheddray ethay onepray artyr’smay emainsray!

Ethay anglingstray erohay angspray upay ithway aay elievingray ortsnay. Erethay asway aay izwhay
asay ofay aay issilemay inay ethay airay, ingledmay ithway ethay urmurmay ofay aay ursecay, aay oundsay
asay ofay iveringshay assglay ollowedfay, anday aay allsmay, aguevay ormfay entway overay ethay
encefay anday otshay awayay inay ethay oomglay.

Otnay onglay afteray, asay Omtay, allay undresseday orfay edbay, asway urveyingsay ishay
encheddray armentsgay byay ethay ightlay ofay aay allowtay ipday, Idsay okeway upay; utbay ifay ehay
adhay anyay imday ideaay ofay akingmay anyay eferences“ray otay allusions”ay, ehay oughtthay
etterbay ofay itay anday eldhay ishay eacepay, orfay erethay asway angerday inay Om’stay eyeay.

Omtay urnedtay inay ithoutway ethay addeday exationvay ofay ayerspray, anday Idsay ademay entalmay
otenay ofay ethay omissionay.




APTERchay IVay


Ethay unsay oseray uponay aay anquiltray orldway, anday eamedbay ownday uponay ethay eacefulpay
illagevay ikelay aay enedictionbay. Eakfastbray overay, Auntay Ollypay adhay amilyfay
orshipway: itay eganbay ithway aay ayerpray uiltbay omfray ethay oundgray upay ofay olidsay
oursescay ofay Ipturalscray uotationsqay, eldedway ogethertay ithway aay inthay ortarmay ofay

Inay ueday oursecay ethay uperintendentsay oodstay upay inay ontfray ofay ethay ulpitpay, ithway

eaveslay, anday ommandedcay attentionay. Enwhay aay Unday-schoolsay uperintendentsay
akesmay ishay ustomarycay ittlelay eechspay, aay ookhymn-bay inay ethay andhay isay asay

isay everay eferredray otay byay ethay ufferersay. Isthay uperintendentsay asway aay imslay

encefay atthay ompelledcay aay aightstray ookoutlay aheaday, anday aay urningtay ofay ethay
olewhay odybay enwhay aay idesay iewvay asway equiredray; ishay inchay asway oppedpray onay aay

ingedfray endsay; ishay ootbay oestay ereway urnedtay arplyshay upay, inay ethay ashionfay

oducedpray byay ethay oungyay enmay byay ittingsay ithway eirthay oestay essedpray againstay aay
allway orfay ourshay ogethertay. Mray. Altersway asway eryvay earnestay ofay ienmay, anday eryvay
inceresay anday onesthay atay earthay; anday ehay eldhay acredsay ingsthay anday acesplay

ashionfay:

ow“nay, ildrenchay, Iay antway ouyay allay otay itsay upay ustjay asay aightstray anday ettypray asay
ouyay ancay anday ivegay emay allay ouryay attentionay orfay aay inutemay oray otway. Ere—thatthay
isay itay. Atthay isay ethay ayway oodgay ittlelay oysbay anday irlsgay ouldshay oday. Iay eesay oneay
ittlelay irlgay owhay isay ookinglay outay ofay ethay indow—Iway amay afraiday eshay inksthay Iay
amay outay erethay omewhere—perhapssay upay inay oneay ofay ethay eestray akingmay aay eechspay
otay ethay ittlelay irdsbay. Applausive[ay itter]tay. Iay antway otay elltay ouyay owhay oodgay itay
akesmay emay eelfay otay eesay osay anymay ightbray, eanclay ittlelay acesfay assembleday inay aay
aceplay ikelay isthay, earninglay otay oday ightray anday ebay ood”gay. Anday osay orthfay anday osay
onay. Itay isay otnay ecessarynay otay etsay ownday ethay estray ofay ethay orationay. Itay asway ofay aay
atternpay ichwhay oesday otnay aryvay, anday osay itay isay amiliarfay otay usay allay.

Ethay atterlay irdthay ofay ethay eechspay asway arredmay byay ethay esumptionray ofay ightsfay
anday otheray ecreationsray amongay ertaincay ofay ethay adbay oysbay, anday byay idgetingsfay
anday isperingswhay atthay extendeday arfay anday ideway, ashingway evenay otay ethay asesbay ofay
isolateday anday incorruptibleay ocksray ikelay Idsay anday Arymay. Utbay ownay everyay oundsay
easedcay uddenlysay, ithway ethay ubsidencesay ofay Mray. Alters’way oicevay, anday ethay
onclusioncay ofay ethay eechspay asway eceivedray ithway aay urstbay ofay ilentsay atitudegray.

Aay oodgay artpay ofay ethay isperingwhay adhay eenbay occasioneday byay anay eventay ichwhay asway
oremay oray esslay are—theray entranceay ofay isitorsvay: awyerlay Atcherthay, accompanieday
byay aay eryvay eeblefay anday ageday anmay; aay inefay, ortlypay, iddle-agedmay entlemangay
ithway iron-grayay airhay; anday aay ignifiedday adylay owhay asway oubtlessday ethay atter’slay
ifeway. Ethay adylay asway eadinglay aay ildchay. Omtay adhay eenbay estlessray anday ullfay ofay
afingschay anday epiningsray; onscience-smittencay, oo—hetay ouldcay otnay eetmay Amyay
Awrence’slay eyeay, ehay ouldcay otnay ookbray erhay ovinglay azegay. Utbay enwhay ehay awsay isthay
allsmay ewcomernay ishay oulsay asway allay ablazeay ithway issblay inay aay omentmay. Ethay extnay
omentmay ehay asway owing“shay off”ay ithway allay ishay ight—cuffingmay oysbay, ullingpay
airhay, akingmay aces—infay aay ordway, usingay everyay artay atthay eemedsay ikelylay otay
ascinatefay aay irlgay anday inway erhay applauseay. Ishay exaltationay adhay utbay oneay
alloy—theay emorymay ofay ishay umiliationhay inay isthay angel’say arden—andgay atthay
ecordray inay andsay asway astfay ashingway outay, underay ethay avesway ofay appinesshay atthay
ereway eepingsway overay itay ownay.

Ethay isitorsvay ereway ivengay ethay ighesthay eatsay ofay onorhay, anday asay oonsay asay Mray.
Alters’way eechspay asway inishedfay, ehay introduceday emthay otay ethay oolschay. Ethay
iddle-agedmay anmay urnedtay outay otay ebay aay odigiouspray ersonage—nopay esslay aay oneay
anthay ethay ountycay udge—altogetherjay ethay ostmay augustay eationcray esethay ildrenchay
adhay everay ookedlay upon—anday eythay onderedway atwhay indkay ofay aterialmay ehay asway ademay
of—anday eythay alfhay antedway otay earhay imhay oarray, anday ereway alfhay afraiday ehay ightmay,
ootay. Ehay asway omfray Onstantinoplecay, elvetway ilesmay away—soay ehay adhay avelledtray,
anday eensay ethay orld—theseway eryvay eyesay adhay ookedlay uponay ethay ountycay
ourt-house—whichcay asway aidsay otay avehay aay intay oofray. Ethay aweay ichwhay esethay
eflectionsray inspireday asway attesteday byay ethay impressiveay ilencesay anday ethay

eirthay ownay awyerlay. Effjay Atcherthay immediatelyay entway orwardfay, otay ebay amiliarfay
ithway ethay eatgray anmay anday ebay envieday byay ethay oolschay. Itay ouldway avehay eenbay usicmay
otay ishay oulsay otay earhay ethay isperingswhay:

ook“lay atay imhay, Imjay! E’shay aay oinggay upay erethay. Ay—looksay! e’shay aay oinggay otay
akeshay andshay ithway im—hehay is__ay akingshay andshay ithway imhay! Byay ingsjay, on’tday ouyay

Mray. Altersway ellfay otay owing“shay off”ay, ithway allay ortssay ofay officialay ustlingsbay
anday activitiesay, ivinggay ordersay, eliveringday udgmentsjay, ischargingday
irectionsday erehay, erethay, everywhereay atthay ehay ouldcay indfay aay argettay. Ethay
ibrarianlay owed“shay off”—runningay itherhay anday itherthay ithway ishay armsay ullfay ofay
ooksbay anday akingmay aay ealday ofay ethay uttersplay anday ussfay atthay insectay authorityay
elightsday inay. Ethay oungyay adylay eacherstay owed“shay off”—bendingay eetlysway overay
upilspay atthay ereway atelylay eingbay oxedbay, iftinglay ettypray arningway ingersfay
atay adbay ittlelay oysbay anday attingpay oodgay onesay ovinglylay. Ethay oungyay entlemengay
eacherstay owed“shay off”ay ithway allsmay oldingsscay anday otheray ittlelay isplaysday ofay
authorityay anday inefay attentionay otay iscipline—andday ostmay ofay ethay eacherstay, ofay
othbay exessay, oundfay usinessbay upay atay ethay ibrarylay, byay ethay ulpitpay; anday itay asway
usinessbay atthay equentlyfray adhay otay ebay oneday overay againay otway oray eethray imestay
ith(way uchmay eemingsay exation)vay. Ethay ittlelay irlsgay owed“shay off”ay inay ariousvay
aysway, anday ethay ittlelay oysbay owed“shay off”ay ithway uchsay iligenceday atthay ethay airay
asway ickthay ithway aperpay adsway anday ethay urmurmay ofay ufflingsscay. Anday aboveay itay
allay ethay eatgray anmay atsay anday eamedbay aay ajesticmay udicialjay ilesmay uponay allay
ethay ousehay, anday armedway imselfhay inay ethay unsay ofay ishay ownay andeur—forgray ehay asway
owing“shay off”ay, ootay.

Erethay asway onlyay oneay ingthay antingway otay akemay Mray. Alters’way ecstasyay ompletecay,
anday atthay asway aay ancechay otay eliverday aay Ible-prizebay anday exhibitay aay odigypray.
Everalsay upilspay adhay aay ewfay ellowyay icketstay, utbay onenay adhay enough—heay adhay eenbay
arounday amongay ethay arstay upilspay inquiringay. Ehay ouldway avehay ivengay orldsway, ownay,
otay avehay atthay Ermangay adlay ackbay againay ithway aay oundsay indmay.

Anday ownay atay isthay omentmay, enwhay opehay asway eadday, Omtay Awyersay amecay orwardfay ithway
inenay ellowyay icketstay, inenay edray icketstay, anday entay ueblay onesay, anday emandedday
aay Iblebay. Isthay asway aay underboltthay outay ofay aay earclay skyay. Altersway asway otnay
expectingay anay applicationay omfray isthay ourcesay orfay ethay extnay entay earsyay. Utbay
erethay asway onay ettinggay arounday it—hereay ereway ethay ertifiedcay eckschay, anday eythay
ereway oodgay orfay eirthay acefay. Omtay asway ereforethay elevateday otay aay aceplay ithway
ethay Udgejay anday ethay otheray electay, anday ethay eatgray ewsnay asway announceday omfray
eadquartershay. Itay asway ethay ostmay unningstay urprisesay ofay ethay ecadeday, anday
osay ofoundpray asway ethay ensationsay atthay itay iftedlay ethay ewnay erohay upay otay ethay
udicialjay one’say altitudeay, anday ethay oolschay adhay otway arvelsmay otay azegay uponay
inay aceplay ofay oneay. Ethay oysbay ereway allay eatenay upay ithway envy—butay osethay atthay
ufferedsay ethay itterestbay angspay ereway osethay owhay erceivedpay ootay atelay atthay eythay
emselvesthay adhay ontributedcay otay isthay atedhay endorsplay byay adingtray icketstay otay
Omtay orfay ethay ealthway ehay adhay amasseday inay ellingsay itewashingwhay ivilegespray.
Esethay espisedday emselvesthay, asay eingbay ethay upesday ofay aay ilyway audfray, aay
uilefulgay akesnay inay ethay assgray.

Ethay izepray asway eliveredday otay Omtay ithway asay uchmay effusionay asay ethay
uperintendentsay ouldcay umppay upay underay ethay ircumstancescay; utbay itay ackedlay
omewhatsay ofay ethay uetray ushgay, orfay ethay oorpay ellow’sfay instinctay aughttay imhay
atthay erethay asway aay erymystay erehay atthay ouldcay otnay ellway earbay ethay ightlay,
erhapspay; itay asway implysay eposterouspray atthay isthay oybay adhay arehousedway otway
ousandthay eavesshay ofay Ipturalscray isdomway onay ishay emises—apray ozenday ouldway
ainstray ishay apacitycay, ithoutway aay oubtday.

Amyay Awrencelay asway oudpray anday adglay, anday eshay iedtray otay akemay Omtay eesay itay inay
erhay ace—butfay ehay ouldn’tway ooklay. Eshay onderedway; enthay eshay asway ustjay aay aingray
oubledtray; extnay aay imday uspicionsay amecay anday ent—cameway againay; eshay atchedway;
aay urtivefay anceglay oldtay erhay orlds—andway enthay erhay earthay okebray, anday eshay asway
ealousjay, anday angryay, anday ethay earstay amecay anday eshay atedhay everybodyay. Omtay ostmay
ofay allay e(shay ought)thay.

Omtay asway introduceday otay ethay Udgejay; utbay ishay onguetay asway iedtay, ishay eathbray
ouldway ardlyhay omecay, ishay earthay uaked—partlyqay ecausebay ofay ethay awfulay
eatnessgray ofay ethay anmay, utbay ainlymay ecausebay ehay asway erhay arentpay. Ehay ouldway
avehay ikedlay otay allfay ownday anday orshipway imhay, ifay itay ereway inay ethay arkday. Ethay
Udgejay utpay ishay andhay onay Om’stay eadhay anday alledcay imhay aay inefay ittlelay anmay, anday
askeday imhay atwhay ishay amenay asway. Ethay oybay ammeredstay, aspedgay, anday otgay itay outay:

om”“tay.

Oh“ay, onay, otnay Om—ittay is—”ay

omas”“thay.

Ah“ay, at’sthay itay. Iay oughtthay erethay asway oremay otay itay, aybemay. At’sthay eryvay ellway.
Utbay ou’veyay anotheray oneay Iay aresayday, anday ou’llyay elltay itay otay emay, on’tway ou”yay?

ell“tay ethay entlemangay ouryay otheray amenay, Omas”thay, aidsay Altersway, and“ay aysay
irsay. Ouyay ustn’tmay orgetfay ouryay anners”may.

omas“thay Awyer—sir”say.

at’s“thay itay! At’sthay aay oodgay oybay. Inefay oybay. Inefay, anlymay ittlelay ellowfay. Otway
ousandthay ersesvay isay aay eatgray any—verymay, eryvay eatgray anymay. Anday ouyay evernay ancay
ebay orrysay orfay ethay oubletray ouyay ooktay otay earnlay emthay; orfay owledgeknay isay orthway
oremay anthay anythingay erethay isay inay ethay orldway; it’say atwhay akesmay eatgray enmay
anday oodgay enmay; ou’llyay ebay aay eatgray anmay anday aay oodgay anmay ourselfyay, omesay
ayday, Omasthay, anday enthay ou’llyay ooklay ackbay anday aysay, It’say allay owingay otay ethay
eciouspray Unday-schoolsay ivilegespray ofay myay oyhood—it’sbay allay owingay otay
myay earday eacherstay atthay aughttay emay otay earn—it’slay allay owingay otay ethay oodgay
uperintendentsay, owhay encourageday emay, anday atchedway overay emay, anday avegay emay aay
eautifulbay Ible—abay endidsplay elegantay Ible—tobay eepkay anday avehay itay allay orfay myay
ownay, always—it’say allay owingay otay ightray ingingbray upay! Atthay isay atwhay ouyay illway
aysay, Omas—andthay ouyay ouldn’tway aketay anyay oneymay orfay osethay otway ousandthay
erses—novay indeeday ouyay ouldn’tway. Anday ownay ouyay ouldn’tway indmay ellingtay emay anday
isthay adylay omesay ofay ethay ingsthay ou’veyay earned—nolay, Iay owknay ouyay ouldn’t—forway
eway areay oudpray ofay ittlelay oysbay atthay earnlay. Ownay, onay oubtday ouyay owknay ethay amesnay
ofay allay ethay elvetway isciplesday. On’tway ouyay elltay usay ethay amesnay ofay ethay irstfay
otway atthay ereway appointed”ay?

Omtay asway uggingtay atay aay utton-holebay anday ookinglay eepishshay. Ehay ushedblay,
ownay, anday ishay eyesay ellfay. Mray. Alters’way earthay anksay ithinway imhay. Ehay aidsay
otay imselfhay, itay isay otnay ossiblepay atthay ethay oybay ancay answeray ethay implestsay
uestion—whyqay id__day ethay Udgejay askay imhay? Etyay ehay eltfay obligeday otay eakspay upay
anday aysay:

Etlay usay awdray ethay urtaincay ofay aritychay overay ethay estray ofay ethay enescay.




APTERchay Vay


Aboutay alf-pasthay entay ethay ackedcray ellbay ofay ethay allsmay urchchay eganbay otay ingray,
anday esentlypray ethay eoplepay eganbay otay athergay orfay ethay orningmay ermonsay. Ethay
Unday-schoolsay ildrenchay istributedday emselvesthay aboutay ethay ousehay anday
occupieday ewspay ithway eirthay arentspay, osay asay otay ebay underay upervisionsay. Auntay
Ollypay amecay, anday Omtay anday Idsay anday Arymay atsay ithway er—Tomhay eingbay acedplay extnay
ethay aisleay, inay orderay atthay ehay ightmay ebay asay arfay awayay omfray ethay openay indowway
anday ethay eductivesay outsideay ummersay enesscay asay ossiblepay. Ethay owdcray iledfay upay
ethay aislesay: ethay ageday anday eedynay ostmasterpay, owhay adhay eensay etterbay aysday;
ethay ayormay anday ishay ife—forway eythay adhay aay ayormay erethay, amongay otheray
unnecessariesay; ethay usticejay ofay ethay eacepay; ethay idowway Ouglasday, airfay,
artsmay, anday ortyfay, aay enerousgay, ood-heartedgay oulsay anday ell-to-doway, erhay illhay
ansionmay ethay onlyay alacepay inay ethay owntay, anday ethay ostmay ospitablehay anday uchmay
ethay ostmay avishlay inay ethay attermay ofay estivitiesfay atthay Stay. Etersburgpay ouldcay
oastbay; ethay entbay anday enerablevay Ajormay anday Mrsay. Ardway; awyerlay Iversonray, ethay
ewnay otablenay omfray aay istanceday; extnay ethay ellebay ofay ethay illagevay, ollowedfay byay
aay ooptray ofay awn-cladlay anday ibbon-deckedray oungyay eart-breakershay; enthay allay
ethay oungyay erksclay inay owntay inay aay ody—forbay eythay adhay oodstay inay ethay estibulevay
uckingsay eirthay ane-headscay, aay irclingcay allway ofay oileday anday imperingsay
admirersay, illtay ethay astlay irlgay adhay unray eirthay antletgay; anday astlay ofay allay amecay
ethay Odelmay Oybay, Illieway Uffersonmay, akingtay asay eedfulhay arecay ofay ishay othermay asay
ifay eshay ereway utcay assglay. Ehay alwaysay oughtbray ishay othermay otay urchchay, anday asway
ethay idepray ofay allay ethay atronsmay. Ethay oysbay allay atedhay imhay, ehay asway osay
oodgay. Anday esidesbay, ehay adhay eenbay own“thray upay otay em”thay osay uchmay. Ishay
itewhay andkerchiefhay asway anginghay outay ofay ishay ocketpay ehindbay, asay usualay onay
Undays—accidentallysay. Omtay adhay onay andkerchiefhay, anday ehay ookedlay uponay oysbay
owhay adhay asay obssnay.

Ethay ongregationcay eingbay ullyfay assembleday, ownay, ethay ellbay angray onceay oremay,
otay arnway aggardslay anday agglersstray, anday enthay aay olemnsay ushhay ellfay uponay ethay
urchchay ichwhay asway onlyay okenbray byay ethay itteringtay anday isperingwhay ofay ethay
oirchay inay ethay allerygay. Ethay oirchay alwaysay itteredtay anday isperedwhay allay
oughthray ervicesay. Erethay asway onceay aay urchchay oirchay atthay asway otnay ill-breday,
utbay Iay avehay orgottenfay erewhay itay asway, ownay. Itay asway aay eatgray anymay earsyay agoay,
anday Iay ancay arcelyscay ememberray anythingay aboutay itay, utbay Iay inkthay itay asway inay
omesay oreignfay ountrycay.

Ethay inistermay avegay outay ethay hymnay, anday eadray itay oughthray ithway aay elishray, inay aay
eculiarpay estylay ichwhay asway uchmay admireday inay atthay artpay ofay ethay ountrycay. Ishay
oicevay eganbay onay aay ediummay eykay anday imbedclay eadilystay upay illtay itay eachedray aay
ertaincay ointpay, erewhay itay orebay ithway ongstray emphasisay uponay ethay opmosttay ordway
anday enthay ungedplay ownday asay ifay omfray aay ing-boardspray:

Allshay Iay ebay ar-ri-edcay oetay ethay iesskay, onay ow’ryflay eds__bay
ofay easeay,

Ilstwhay othersay ightfay otay inway ethay izepray, anday ailsay o’thray ood__blay
-yay eassay?

Ehay asway egardedray asay aay onderfulway eaderray. Atay urchchay ociables”“say ehay asway
alwaysay alledcay uponay otay eadray oetrypay; anday enwhay ehay asway oughthray, ethay adieslay
ouldway iftlay upay eirthay andshay anday etlay emthay allfay elplesslyhay inay eirthay apslay,
anday all”“way eirthay eyesay, anday akeshay eirthay eadshay, asay uchmay asay otay aysay, ords“way
annotcay expressay itay; itay isay ootay eautifulbay, OOtay eautifulbay orfay isthay ortalmay
earth”ay.

Afteray ethay hymnay adhay eenbay ungsay, ethay Evray. Mray. Aguespray urnedtay imselfhay intoay
aay ulletin-boardbay, anday eadray offay otices”“nay ofay eetingsmay anday ocietiessay anday
ingsthay illtay itay eemedsay atthay ethay istlay ouldway etchstray outay otay ethay ackcray ofay
oom—aday ueerqay ustomcay ichwhay isay illstay eptkay upay inay Americaay, evenay inay itiescay,
awayay erehay inay isthay ageay ofay abundantay ewspapersnay. Oftenay, ethay esslay erethay isay
otay ustifyjay aay aditionaltray ustomcay, ethay arderhay itay isay otay etgay idray ofay itay.

Anday ownay ethay inistermay ayedpray. Aay oodgay, enerousgay ayerpray itay asway, anday entway
intoay etailsday: itay eadedplay orfay ethay urchchay, anday ethay ittlelay ildrenchay ofay ethay
urchchay; orfay ethay otheray urcheschay ofay ethay illagevay; orfay ethay illagevay itselfay;
orfay ethay ountycay; orfay ethay Atestay; orfay ethay Atestay officersay; orfay ethay Uniteday
Atesstay; orfay ethay urcheschay ofay ethay Uniteday Atesstay; orfay Ongresscay; orfay ethay
Esidentpray; orfay ethay officersay ofay ethay Overnmentgay; orfay oorpay ailorssay, ossedtay
byay ormystay eassay; orfay ethay oppresseday illionsmay oaninggray underay ethay eelhay ofay
Europeanay onarchiesmay anday Orientalay espotismsday; orfay uchsay asay avehay ethay ightlay
anday ethay oodgay idingstay, anday etyay avehay otnay eyesay otay eesay ornay earsay otay earhay
ithalway; orfay ethay eathenhay inay ethay arfay islandsay ofay ethay easay; anday osedclay ithway
aay upplicationsay atthay ethay ordsway ehay asway aboutay otay eakspay ightmay indfay acegray
anday avorfay, anday ebay asay eedsay ownsay inay ertilefay oundgray, ieldingyay inay imetay aay
atefulgray arvesthay ofay oodgay. Amenay.

Erethay asway aay ustlingray ofay essesdray, anday ethay andingstay ongregationcay atsay ownday.
Ethay oybay osewhay istoryhay isthay ookbay elatesray idday otnay enjoyay ethay ayerpray, ehay
onlyay endureday it—ifay ehay evenay idday atthay uchmay. Ehay asway estiveray allay oughthray itay;
ehay eptkay allytay ofay ethay etailsday ofay ethay ayerpray, unconsciously—foray ehay asway otnay
isteninglay, utbay ehay ewknay ethay oundgray ofay olday, anday ethay ergyman’sclay egularray
outeray overay it—anday enwhay aay ittlelay ifletray ofay ewnay attermay asway interlardeday,
ishay earay etectedday itay anday ishay olewhay aturenay esentedray itay; ehay onsideredcay
additionsay unfairay, anday oundrellyscay. Inay ethay idstmay ofay ethay ayerpray aay flyay adhay
itlay onay ethay ackbay ofay ethay ewpay inay ontfray ofay imhay anday orturedtay ishay iritspay byay
almlycay ubbingray itsay andshay ogethertay, embracingay itsay eadhay ithway itsay armsay, anday
olishingpay itay osay igorouslyvay atthay itay eemedsay otay almostay artpay ompanycay ithway
ethay odybay, anday ethay enderslay eadthray ofay aay ecknay asway exposeday otay iewvay; apingscray
itsay ingsway ithway itsay indhay egslay anday oothingsmay emthay otay itsay odybay asay ifay eythay
adhay eenbay oat-tailscay; oinggay oughthray itsay olewhay oilettay asay anquillytray asay ifay
itay ewknay itay asway erfectlypay afesay. Asay indeeday itay asway; orfay asay orelysay asay Om’stay
andshay itcheday otay abgray orfay itay eythay idday otnay are—heday elievedbay ishay oulsay ouldway
ebay instantlyay estroyedday ifay ehay idday uchsay aay ingthay ilewhay ethay ayerpray asway oinggay
onay. Utbay ithway ethay osingclay entencesay ishay andhay eganbay otay urvecay anday ealstay
orwardfay; anday ethay instantay ethay Amen”“ay asway outay ethay flyay asway aay isonerpray ofay
arway. Ishay auntay etectedday ethay actay anday ademay imhay etlay itay ogay.

Ethay inistermay avegay outay ishay exttay anday oneddray alongay onotonouslymay oughthray anay
argumentay atthay asway osay osypray atthay anymay aay eadhay byay anday byay eganbay otay od—andnay
etyay itay asway anay argumentay atthay ealtday inay imitlesslay irefay anday imstonebray anday
innedthay ethay edestinedpray electay ownday otay aay ompanycay osay allsmay asay otay ebay ardlyhay
orthway ethay avingsay. Omtay ountedcay ethay agespay ofay ethay ermonsay; afteray urchchay ehay
alwaysay ewknay owhay anymay agespay erethay adhay eenbay, utbay ehay eldomsay ewknay anythingay
elseay aboutay ethay iscourseday. Oweverhay, isthay imetay ehay asway eallyray interesteday
orfay aay ittlelay ilewhay. Ethay inistermay ademay aay andgray anday ovingmay icturepay ofay ethay
assemblingay ogethertay ofay ethay orld’sway ostshay atay ethay illenniummay enwhay ethay ionlay
anday ethay amblay ouldshay ielay ownday ogethertay anday aay ittlelay ildchay ouldshay eadlay
emthay. Utbay ethay athospay, ethay essonlay, ethay oralmay ofay ethay eatgray ectaclespay
ereway ostlay uponay ethay oybay; ehay onlyay oughtthay ofay ethay onspicuousnesscay ofay ethay
incipalpray aracterchay eforebay ethay on-lookingay ationsnay; ishay acefay itlay ithway ethay
oughtthay, anday ehay aidsay otay imselfhay atthay ehay ishedway ehay ouldcay ebay atthay ildchay,
ifay itay asway aay ametay ionlay.

Ownay ehay apsedlay intoay ufferingsay againay, asay ethay dryay argumentay asway esumedray.
Esentlypray ehay ethoughtbay imhay ofay aay easuretray ehay adhay anday otgay itay outay. Itay asway
aay argelay ackblay eetlebay ithway ormidablefay aws—ajay inchbug”“pay, ehay alledcay itay. Itay
asway inay aay ercussion-cappay oxbay. Ethay irstfay ingthay ethay eetlebay idday asway otay
aketay imhay byay ethay ingerfay. Aay aturalnay illipfay ollowedfay, ethay eetlebay entway
ounderingflay intoay ethay aisleay anday itlay onay itsay ackbay, anday ethay urthay ingerfay entway
intoay ethay oy’sbay outhmay. Ethay eetlebay aylay erethay orkingway itsay elplesshay egslay,
unableay otay urntay overay. Omtay eyeday itay, anday ongedlay orfay itay; utbay itay asway afesay outay
ofay ishay eachray. Otheray eoplepay uninteresteday inay ethay ermonsay oundfay eliefray inay
ethay eetlebay, anday eythay eyeday itay ootay. Esentlypray aay agrantvay oodlepay ogday amecay
idlingay alongay, adsay atay earthay, azylay ithway ethay ummersay oftnesssay anday ethay
uietqay, earyway ofay aptivitycay, ighingsay orfay angechay. Ehay iedspay ethay eetlebay; ethay
oopingdray ailtay iftedlay anday aggedway. Ehay urveyedsay ethay izepray; alkedway arounday
itay; eltsmay atay itay omfray aay afesay istanceday; alkedway arounday itay againay; ewgray
olderbay, anday ooktay aay oserclay ellsmay; enthay iftedlay ishay iplay anday ademay aay ingerlygay
atchsnay atay itay, ustjay issingmay itay; ademay anotheray, anday anotheray; eganbay otay enjoyay
ethay iversionday; ubsidedsay otay ishay omachstay ithway ethay eetlebay etweenbay ishay awspay,
anday ontinuedcay ishay experimentsay; ewgray earyway atay astlay, anday enthay indifferentay
anday absent-mindeday. Ishay eadhay oddednay, anday ittlelay byay ittlelay ishay inchay
escendedday anday ouchedtay ethay enemyay, owhay eizedsay itay. Erethay asway aay arpshay elpyay,
aay irtflay ofay ethay oodle’spay eadhay, anday ethay eetlebay ellfay aay ouplecay ofay ardsyay
awayay, anday itlay onay itsay ackbay onceay oremay. Ethay eighboringnay ectatorsspay
ookshay ithway aay entlegay inwarday oyjay, everalsay acesfay entway ehindbay ansfay anday
and-kerchiefshay, anday Omtay asway entirelyay appyhay. Ethay ogday ookedlay oolishfay,
anday obablypray eltfay osay; utbay erethay asway esentmentray inay ishay earthay, ootay, anday aay
avingcray orfay evengeray. Osay ehay entway otay ethay eetlebay anday eganbay aay aryway attackay onay
itay againay; umpingjay atay itay omfray everyay ointpay ofay aay irclecay, ightinglay ithway ishay
ore-pawsfay ithinway anay inchay ofay ethay eaturecray, akingmay evenay oserclay atchessnay atay
itay ithway ishay eethtay, anday erkingjay ishay eadhay illtay ishay earsay appedflay againay. Utbay
ehay ewgray iredtay onceay oremay, afteray aay ilewhay; iedtray otay amuseay imselfhay ithway aay
flyay utbay oundfay onay eliefray; ollowedfay anay antay arounday, ithway ishay osenay oseclay
otay ethay oorflay, anday uicklyqay eariedway ofay atthay; awnedyay, ighedsay, orgotfay ethay
eetlebay entirelyay, anday atsay ownday onay itay. Enthay erethay asway aay ildway elpyay ofay agonyay
anday ethay oodlepay entway ailingsay upay ethay aisleay; ethay elpsyay ontinuedcay, anday osay
idday ethay ogday; ehay ossedcray ethay ousehay inay ontfray ofay ethay altaray; ehay ewflay
ownday ethay otheray aisleay; ehay ossedcray eforebay ethay oorsday; ehay amoredclay upay ethay
ome-stretchhay; ishay anguishay ewgray ithway ishay ogresspray, illtay esentlypray ehay asway
utbay aay oollyway ometcay ovingmay inay itsay orbitay ithway ethay eamglay anday ethay eedspay ofay
ightlay. Atay astlay ethay anticfray ufferersay eeredshay omfray itsay oursecay, anday angspray
intoay itsay aster’smay aplay; ehay ungflay itay outay ofay ethay indowway, anday ethay oicevay ofay
istressday uicklyqay innedthay awayay anday iedday inay ethay istanceday.

Byay isthay imetay ethay olewhay urchchay asway ed-facedray anday uffocatingsay ithway
uppressedsay aughterlay, anday ethay ermonsay adhay omecay otay aay eadday andstillstay.
Ethay iscourseday asway esumedray esentlypray, utbay itay entway amelay anday altinghay, allay
ossibilitypay ofay impressivenessay eingbay atay anay enday; orfay evenay ethay avestgray
entimentssay ereway onstantlycay eingbay eceivedray ithway aay otheredsmay urstbay ofay
unholyay irthmay, underay overcay ofay omesay emoteray ew-backpay, asay ifay ethay oorpay arsonpay
adhay aidsay aay arelyray acetiousfay ingthay. Itay asway aay enuinegay eliefray otay ethay olewhay
ongregationcay enwhay ethay ordealay asway overay anday ethay enedictionbay onouncedpray.

Omtay Awyersay entway omehay uiteqay eerfulchay, inkingthay otay imselfhay atthay erethay asway
omesay atisfactionsay aboutay ivineday ervicesay enwhay erethay asway aay itbay ofay arietyvay
inay itay. Ehay adhay utbay oneay arringmay oughtthay; ehay asway illingway atthay ethay ogday
ouldshay ayplay ithway ishay inchbugpay, utbay ehay idday otnay inkthay itay asway uprightay inay
imhay otay arrycay itay offay.




APTERchay Ivay


Ondaymay orningmay oundfay Omtay Awyersay iserablemay. Ondaymay orningmay alwaysay oundfay
imhay o—becausesay itay eganbay anotheray eek’sway owslay ufferingsay inay oolschay. Ehay
enerallygay eganbay atthay ayday ithway ishingway ehay adhay adhay onay interveningay olidayhay,
itay ademay ethay oinggay intoay aptivitycay anday ettersfay againay osay uchmay oremay odiousay.

Omtay aylay inkingthay. Esentlypray itay occurreday otay imhay atthay ehay ishedway ehay asway
icksay; enthay ehay ouldcay aystay omehay omfray oolschay. Erehay asway aay aguevay ossibilitypay.
Ehay anvassedcay ishay emsystay. Onay ailmentay asway oundfay, anday ehay investigateday

Ethay aster’smay ulsepay oodstay illstay, anday ehay aredstay elplesslyhay. Ethay uzzbay ofay
udystay easedcay. Ethay upilspay onderedway ifay isthay oolhardyfay oybay adhay ostlay ishay
indmay. Ethay astermay aidsay:

ou—you“yay idday at”whay?

opped“stay otay alktay ithway Uckleberryhay Inn”fay.

Erethay asway onay istakingmay ethay ordsway.

omas“thay Awyersay, isthay isay ethay ostmay astoundingay onfessioncay Iay avehay everay
istenedlay otay. Onay eremay erulefay illway answeray orfay isthay offenceay. Aketay offay ouryay
acket”jay.

Ethay aster’smay armay erformedpay untilay itay asway iredtay anday ethay ockstay ofay itchessway
otablynay iminishedday. Enthay ethay orderay ollowedfay:

ow“nay, irsay, ogay anday itsay ithway ethay irlsgay! Anday etlay isthay ebay aay arningway otay ou”yay.

Ethay ittertay atthay ippledray arounday ethay oomray appeareday otay abashay ethay oybay, utbay
inay ealityray atthay esultray asway ausedcay atherray oremay byay ishay orshipfulway aweay
ofay ishay unknownay idolay anday ethay eaddray easureplay atthay aylay inay ishay ighhay oodgay
ortunefay. Ehay atsay ownday uponay ethay enday ofay ethay inepay enchbay anday ethay irlgay itchedhay
erselfhay awayay omfray imhay ithway aay osstay ofay erhay eadhay. Udgesnay anday inksway anday
isperswhay aversedtray ethay oomray, utbay Omtay atsay illstay, ithway ishay armsay uponay ethay
onglay, owlay eskday eforebay imhay, anday eemedsay otay udystay ishay ookbay.

Byay anday byay attentionay easedcay omfray imhay, anday ethay accustomeday oolschay urmurmay
oseray uponay ethay ullday airay onceay oremay. Esentlypray ethay oybay eganbay otay ealstay
urtivefay ancesglay atay ethay irlgay. Eshay observeday itay, ade“may aay outh”may atay imhay
anday avegay imhay ethay ackbay ofay erhay eadhay orfay ethay acespay ofay aay inutemay. Enwhay eshay
autiouslycay acedfay arounday againay, aay eachpay aylay eforebay erhay. Eshay ustthray itay
awayay. Omtay entlygay utpay itay ackbay. Eshay ustthray itay awayay againay, utbay ithway esslay
animosityay. Omtay atientlypay eturnedray itay otay itsay aceplay. Enthay eshay etlay itay
emainray. Omtay awledscray onay ishay ateslay, ease“play aketay it—Iay otgay ore”may. Ethay
irlgay ancedglay atay ethay ordsway, utbay ademay onay ignsay. Ownay ethay oybay eganbay otay awdray
omethingsay onay ethay ateslay, idinghay ishay orkway ithway ishay eftlay andhay. Orfay aay imetay
ethay irlgay efusedray otay oticenay; utbay erhay umanhay uriositycay esentlypray eganbay
otay anifestmay itselfay byay ardlyhay erceptiblepay ignssay. Ethay oybay orkedway onay,
apparentlyay unconsciousay. Ethay irlgay ademay aay ortsay ofay on-committalnay attemptay
otay eesay, utbay ethay oybay idday otnay etraybay atthay ehay asway awareay ofay itay. Atay astlay eshay
avegay inay anday esitatinglyhay isperedwhay:

et“lay emay eesay it”ay.

Omtay artlypay uncovereday aay ismalday aricaturecay ofay aay ousehay ithway otway ablegay endsay
otay itay anday aay orkscrewcay ofay okesmay issuingay omfray ethay imneychay. Enthay ethay irl’sgay
interestay eganbay otay astenfay itselfay uponay ethay orkway anday eshay orgotfay everythingay
elseay. Enwhay itay asway inishedfay, eshay azedgay aay omentmay, enthay isperedwhay:

It’s“ay ice—makenay aay an”may.

Ethay artistay erecteday aay anmay inay ethay ontfray ardyay, atthay esembledray aay errickday. Ehay
ouldcay avehay eppedstay overay ethay ousehay; utbay ethay irlgay asway otnay ercriticalhypay;
eshay asway atisfiedsay ithway ethay onstermay, anday isperedwhay:

It’s“ay aay eautifulbay an—nowmay akemay emay omingcay along”ay.

Omtay ewdray anay our-glasshay ithway aay ullfay oonmay anday awstray imbslay otay itay anday armeday
ethay eadingspray ingersfay ithway aay ortentouspay anfay. Ethay irlgay aidsay:

It’s“ay everay osay ice—Inay ishway Iay ouldcay aw”dray.

It’s“ay easy”ay, isperedwhay Omtay, I’ll“ay earnlay ou”yay.

Oh“ay, illway ouyay? En”whay?

At“ay oonnay. Oday ouyay ogay omehay otay inner”day?

I’ll“ay aystay ifay ouyay ill”way.

ood—that’s“gay aay ackwhay. At’swhay ouryay ame”nay?

ecky“bay Atcherthay. At’swhay oursyay? Ohay, Iay owknay. It’say Omasthay Awyer”say.

at’s“thay ethay amenay eythay icklay emay byay. I’may Omtay enwhay I’may oodgay. Ouyay allcay emay
Omtay, illway ou”yay?

es”“yay.

Ownay Omtay eganbay otay awlscray omethingsay onay ethay ateslay, idinghay ethay ordsway omfray
ethay irlgay. Utbay eshay asway otnay ackwardbay isthay imetay. Eshay eggedbay otay eesay. Omtay
aidsay:

Oh“ay, itay ain’tay anything”ay.

es“yay itay is”ay.

o“nay itay ain’tay. Ouyay on’tday antway otay ee”say.

es“yay Iay oday, indeeday Iay oday. Easeplay etlay e”may.

ou’ll“yay ell”tay.

o“nay Iay on’t—deedway anday eedday anday oubleday eedday on’t”way.

ou“yay on’tway elltay anybodyay atay allay? Everay, asay onglay asay ouyay ive”lay?

o“nay, Iay on’tway everay elltay any_body_ay. Ownay etlay e”may.

Oh“ay, ou__yay on’tday antway otay ee”say!

ow“nay atthay ouyay eattray emay osay, Iay ill__way ee”say. Anday eshay utpay erhay allsmay andhay
uponay ishay anday aay ittlelay ufflescay ensueday, Omtay etendingpray otay esistray inay
earnestay utbay ettinglay ishay andhay ipslay byay egreesday illtay esethay ordsway ereway
evealedray: I“_ay ovelay ou_”yay.

Oh“ay, ouyay adbay ing”thay! Anday eshay ithay ishay andhay aay artsmay apray, utbay eddenedray anday
ookedlay easedplay, everthelessnay.

Ustjay atay isthay uncturejay ethay oybay eltfay aay owslay, atefulfay ipgray osingclay onay ishay
earay, anday aay eadystay iftinglay impulseay. Inay atthay iseway ehay asway ornebay acrossay ethay
ousehay anday epositedday inay ishay ownay eatsay, underay aay epperingpay irefay ofay igglesgay
omfray ethay olewhay oolschay. Enthay ethay astermay oodstay overay imhay uringday aay ewfay awfulay
omentsmay, anday inallyfay ovedmay awayay otay ishay onethray ithoutway ayingsay aay ordway. Utbay
althoughay Om’stay earay ingledtay, ishay earthay asway ubilantjay.

Asay ethay oolschay uietedqay ownday Omtay ademay anay onesthay effortay otay udystay, utbay
ethay urmoiltay ithinway imhay asway ootay eatgray. Inay urntay ehay ooktay ishay aceplay inay ethay
eadingray assclay anday ademay aay otchbay ofay itay; enthay inay ethay eographygay assclay anday
urnedtay akeslay intoay ountainsmay, ountainsmay intoay iversray, anday iversray intoay
ontinentscay, illtay aoschay asway omecay againay; enthay inay ethay ellingspay assclay, anday
otgay urned“tay own”day, byay aay uccessionsay ofay eremay abybay ordsway, illtay ehay oughtbray
upay atay ethay ootfay anday ieldedyay upay ethay ewterpay edalmay ichwhay ehay adhay ornway ithway
ostentationay orfay onthsmay.




APTERchay IIvay


Ethay arderhay Omtay iedtray otay astenfay ishay indmay onay ishay ookbay, ethay oremay ishay ideasay
anderedway. Osay atay astlay, ithway aay ighsay anday aay awnyay, ehay avegay itay upay. Itay eemedsay
otay imhay atthay ethay oonnay ecessray ouldway evernay omecay. Ethay airay asway utterlyay eadday.
Erethay asway otnay aay eathbray irringstay. Itay asway ethay eepiestslay ofay eepyslay aysday.
Ethay owsingdray urmurmay ofay ethay ivefay anday entytway udyingstay olarsschay oothedsay
ethay oulsay ikelay ethay ellspay atthay isay inay ethay urmurmay ofay eesbay. Awayay offay inay ethay
amingflay unshinesay, Ardiffcay Illhay iftedlay itsay oftsay eengray idessay oughthray aay
immeringshay eilvay ofay eathay, intedtay ithway ethay urplepay ofay istanceday; aay ewfay irdsbay
oatedflay onay azylay ingway ighhay inay ethay airay; onay otheray ivinglay ingthay asway isiblevay
utbay omesay owscay, anday eythay ereway asleepay. Om’stay earthay acheday otay ebay eefray, oray
elseay otay avehay omethingsay ofay interestay otay oday otay asspay ethay earydray imetay.
Ishay andhay anderedway intoay ishay ocketpay anday ishay acefay itlay upay ithway aay owglay ofay
atitudegray atthay asway ayerpray, oughthay ehay idday otnay owknay itay. Enthay urtivelyfay
ethay ercussion-cappay oxbay amecay outay. Ehay eleasedray ethay icktay anday utpay imhay onay
ethay onglay atflay eskday. Ethay eaturecray obablypray owedglay ithway aay atitudegray atthay
amounteday otay ayerpray, ootay, atay isthay omentmay, utbay itay asway ematurepray: orfay enwhay
ehay artedstay ankfullythay otay aveltray offay, Omtay urnedtay imhay asideay ithway aay inpay anday
ademay imhay aketay aay ewnay irectionday.

Om’stay osombay iendfray atsay extnay imhay, ufferingsay ustjay asay Omtay adhay eenbay, anday
ownay ehay asway eeplyday anday atefullygray interesteday inay isthay entertainmentay inay
anay instantay. Isthay osombay iendfray asway Oejay Arperhay. Ethay otway oysbay ereway ornsway
iendsfray allay ethay eekway, anday embattleday enemiesay onay Aturdayssay. Oejay ooktay aay
inpay outay ofay ishay apellay anday eganbay otay assistay inay exercisingay ethay isonerpray.
Ethay ortspay ewgray inay interestay omentlymay. Oonsay Omtay aidsay atthay eythay ereway
interferingay ithway eachay otheray, anday eithernay ettinggay ethay ullestfay enefitbay
ofay ethay icktay. Osay ehay utpay Oe’sjay ateslay onay ethay eskday anday ewdray aay inelay ownday ethay
iddlemay ofay itay omfray optay otay ottombay.

ow”“nay, aidsay ehay, as“ay onglay asay ehay isay onay ouryay idesay ouyay ancay irstay imhay upay anday
I’llay etlay imhay aloneay; utbay ifay ouyay etlay imhay etgay awayay anday etgay onay myay idesay,
ou’reyay otay eavelay imhay aloneay asay onglay asay Iay ancay eepkay imhay omfray ossingcray over”ay.

All“ay ightray, ogay aheaday; artstay imhay up”ay.

Ethay icktay escapeday omfray Omtay, esentlypray, anday ossedcray ethay equatoray. Oejay
arassedhay imhay awhileay, anday enthay ehay otgay awayay anday ossedcray ackbay againay. Isthay
angechay ofay asebay occurreday oftenay. Ilewhay oneay oybay asway orryingway ethay icktay ithway
absorbingay interestay, ethay otheray ouldway ooklay onay ithway interestay asay ongstray, ethay
otway eadshay owedbay ogethertay overay ethay ateslay, anday ethay otway oulssay eadday otay allay
ingsthay elseay. Atay astlay ucklay eemedsay otay ettlesay anday abideay ithway Oejay. Ethay
icktay iedtray isthay, atthay, anday ethay otheray oursecay, anday otgay asay exciteday anday asay
anxiousay asay ethay oysbay emselvesthay, utbay imetay anday againay ustjay asay ehay ouldway
avehay ictoryvay inay ishay eryvay aspgray, osay otay eakspay, anday Om’stay ingersfay ouldway
ebay itchingtway otay eginbay, Oe’sjay inpay ouldway eftlyday eadhay imhay offay, anday eepkay
ossessionpay. Atay astlay Omtay ouldcay andstay itay onay ongerlay. Ethay emptationtay asway ootay
ongstray. Osay ehay eachedray outay anday entlay aay andhay ithway ishay inpay. Oejay asway angryay inay
aay omentmay. Aidsay ehay:

om“tay, ouyay etlay imhay alone”ay.

I“ay onlyay ustjay antway otay irstay imhay upay aay ittlelay, Oe”jay.

o“nay, irsay, itay ain’tay airfay; ouyay ustjay etlay imhay alone”ay.

ame“blay itay, Iay ain’tay oinggay otay irstay imhay uch”may.

et“lay imhay aloneay, Iay elltay ou”yay.

I“ay on’t”way!

ou“yay all—he’sshay onay myay idesay ofay ethay ine”lay.

ook“lay erehay, Oejay Arperhay, osewhay isay atthay ick”tay?

I“ay on’tday arecay osewhay icktay ehay is—he’say onay myay idesay ofay ethay inelay, anday ouyay
a’n’tshay ouchtay im”hay.

ell“way, I’llay ustjay etbay Iay illway, oughthay. E’shay myay icktay anday I’llay oday atwhay Iay
ameblay easeplay ithway imhay, oray ie”day!

Aay emendoustray ackwhay amecay ownday onay Om’stay ouldersshay, anday itsay uplicateday onay
Oe’sjay; anday orfay ethay acespay ofay otway inutesmay ethay ustday ontinuedcay otay flyay omfray
ethay otway acketsjay anday ethay olewhay oolschay otay enjoyay itay. Ethay oysbay adhay eenbay
ootay absorbeday otay oticenay ethay ushhay atthay adhay olenstay uponay ethay oolschay awhileay
eforebay enwhay ethay astermay amecay iptoeingtay ownday ethay oomray anday oodstay overay emthay.
Ehay adhay ontemplatedcay aay oodgay artpay ofay ethay erformancepay eforebay ehay ontributedcay
ishay itbay ofay arietyvay otay itay.

Enwhay oolschay okebray upay atay oonnay, Omtay ewflay otay Eckybay Atcherthay, anday isperedwhay
inay erhay earay:

ut“pay onay ouryay onnetbay anday etlay onay ou’reyay oinggay omehay; anday enwhay ouyay etgay otay
ethay ornercay, ivegay ethay estray ofay em’ay ethay ipslay, anday urntay ownday oughthray ethay
anelay anday omecay ackbay. I’llay ogay ethay otheray ayway anday omecay itay overay em’ay ethay amesay
ay”way.

Osay ethay oneay entway offay ithway oneay oupgray ofay olarsschay, anday ethay otheray ithway
anotheray. Inay aay ittlelay ilewhay ethay otway etmay atay ethay ottombay ofay ethay anelay, anday
enwhay eythay eachedray ethay oolschay eythay adhay itay allay otay emselvesthay. Enthay eythay
atsay ogethertay, ithway aay ateslay eforebay emthay, anday Omtay avegay Eckybay ethay encilpay
anday eldhay erhay andhay inay ishay, uidinggay itay, anday osay eatedcray anotheray urprisingsay
ousehay. Enwhay ethay interestay inay artay eganbay otay aneway, ethay otway ellfay otay alkingtay.
Omtay asway immingsway inay issblay. Ehay aidsay:

o“day ouyay ovelay ats”ray?

o“nay! Iay atehay em”thay!

ell“way, Iay oday, oo—_live_tay onesay. Utbay Iay eanmay eadday onesay, otay ingsway oundray ouryay
eadhay ithway aay ing”stray.

o“nay, Iay on’tday arecay orfay atsray uchmay, anywayay. Atwhay Iay ikelay isay ewing-gum”chay.

Oh“ay, Iay ouldshay aysay osay! Iay ishway Iay adhay omesay ow”nay.

o“day ouyay? I’veay otgay omesay. I’llay etlay ouyay ewchay itay awhileay, utbay ouyay ustmay ivegay
itay ackbay otay e”may.

Atthay asway agreeableay, osay eythay ewedchay itay urntay aboutay, anday angledday eirthay egslay
againstay ethay enchbay inay excessay ofay ontentmentcay.

as“way ouyay everay atay aay ircus”cay? aidsay Omtay.

Oh“ay, areay ouyay! Atthay illway ebay icenay. Ey’rethay osay ovelylay, allay ottedspay up”ay.

o”“nay.

iss“kay? Atwhay oday ouyay isskay or”fay?

Everybody”“ay?

e—yes”“yay.

at“whay asway it”ay?

o“nay, ow”nay.

o“nay, otnay ow—to-morrow”nay.

Oh“ay, onay, ow__nay. Easeplay, Ecky—I’llbay isperwhay itay, I’llay isperwhay itay everay osay
easy”ay.

Eckybay esitatinghay, Omtay ooktay ilencesay orfay onsentcay, anday assedpay ishay armay aboutay
erhay aistway anday isperedwhay ethay aletay everay osay oftlysay, ithway ishay outhmay oseclay otay
erhay earay. Anday enthay ehay addeday:

ow“nay ouyay isperwhay itay otay e—justmay ethay ame”say.

Eshay esistedray, orfay aay ilewhay, anday enthay aidsay:

ou“yay urntay ouryay acefay awayay osay ouyay an’tcay eesay, anday enthay Iay illway. Utbay ouyay
ustn’tmay everay elltay anybody—_will_ay ouyay, Omtay? Ownay ouyay on’tway, ill__way ou”yay?

o“nay, indeeday, indeeday Iay on’tway. Ownay, Ecky”bay.

Ehay urnedtay ishay acefay awayay. Eshay entbay imidlytay arounday illtay erhay eathbray irredstay
ishay urlscay anday isperedwhay, I—love—you”“ay!

Enthay eshay angspray awayay anday anray arounday anday arounday ethay esksday anday enchesbay,
ithway Omtay afteray erhay, anday ooktay efugeray inay aay ornercay atay astlay, ithway erhay ittlelay
itewhay apronay otay erhay acefay. Omtay aspedclay erhay aboutay erhay ecknay anday eadedplay:

ow“nay, Eckybay, it’say allay one—allday overay utbay ethay isskay. On’tday ouyay ebay afraiday
ofay at—itthay ain’tay anythingay atay allay. Easeplay, Ecky”bay. Anday ehay uggedtay atay erhay
apronay anday ethay andshay.

Byay anday byay eshay avegay upay, anday etlay erhay andshay opdray; erhay acefay, allay owingglay
ithway ethay ugglestray, amecay upay anday ubmittedsay. Omtay issedkay ethay edray ipslay anday
aidsay:

ow“nay it’say allay oneday, Eckybay. Anday alwaysay afteray isthay, ouyay owknay, ouyay ain’tay
everay otay ovelay anybodyay utbay emay, anday ouyay ain’tay everay otay arrymay anybodyay utbay emay,
everay evernay anday oreverfay. Illway ou”yay?

o“nay, I’llay evernay ovelay anybodyay utbay ouyay, Omtay, anday I’llay evernay arrymay anybodyay
utbay ou—andyay ouyay ain’tay otay everay arrymay anybodyay utbay emay, either”ay.

ertainly“cay. Ofay oursecay. At’sthay art__pay ofay itay. Anday alwaysay omingcay otay oolschay
oray enwhay e’reway oinggay omehay, ou’reyay otay alkway ithway emay, enwhay erethay ain’tay
anybodyay ooking—andlay ouyay oosechay emay anday Iay oosechay ouyay atay artiespay, ecausebay
at’sthay ethay ayway ouyay oday enwhay ou’reyay engaged”ay.

It’s“ay osay icenay. Iay evernay eardhay ofay itay efore”bay.

Oh“ay, it’say everay osay aygay! Whyay, emay anday Amyay Awrence—”lay

Ethay igbay eyesay oldtay Omtay ishay underblay anday ehay oppedstay, onfusedcay.

Oh“ay, Omtay! Enthay Iay ain’tay ethay irstfay ou’veyay everay eenbay engageday o”tay!

Ethay ildchay eganbay otay cryay. Omtay aidsay:

Oh“ay, on’tday cryay, Eckybay, Iay on’tday arecay orfay erhay anyay ore”may.

es“yay, ouyay oday, Om—youtay owknay ouyay o”day.

Omtay iedtray otay utpay ishay armay aboutay erhay ecknay, utbay eshay ushedpay imhay awayay anday
urnedtay erhay acefay otay ethay allway, anday entway onay ingcryay. Omtay iedtray againay, ithway
oothingsay ordsway inay ishay outhmay, anday asway epulsedray againay. Enthay ishay idepray asway
upay, anday ehay odestray awayay anday entway outsideay. Ehay oodstay aboutay, estlessray anday
uneasyay, orfay aay ilewhay, ancingglay atay ethay oorday, everyay ownay anday enthay, opinghay
eshay ouldway epentray anday omecay otay indfay imhay. Utbay eshay idday otnay. Enthay ehay eganbay
otay eelfay adlybay anday earfay atthay ehay asway inay ethay ongwray. Itay asway aay ardhay ugglestray
ithway imhay otay akemay ewnay advancesay, ownay, utbay ehay ervednay imselfhay otay itay anday
entereday. Eshay asway illstay andingstay ackbay erethay inay ethay ornercay, obbingsay, ithway
erhay acefay otay ethay allway. Om’stay earthay otesmay imhay. Ehay entway otay erhay anday oodstay aay
omentmay, otnay owingknay exactlyay owhay otay oceedpray. Enthay ehay aidsay esitatinglyhay:

ecky“bay, I—Iay on’tday arecay orfay anybodyay utbay ou”yay.

Onay eply—butray obssay.

ecky”—pleadingly“bay. ecky“bay, on’tway ouyay aysay omething”say?

APTERchay IIIvay

eanclay Unday-schoolsay ecordray ehay ouldcay ebay illingway otay ogay, anday ebay oneday ithway
itay allay. Ownay asay otay isthay irlgay. Atwhay adhay ehay oneday? Othingnay. Ehay adhay eantmay

ieday emporarily__tay!
