APTERchay IXay


Atay alf-pasthay inenay, atthay ightnay, Omtay anday Idsay ereway entsay otay edbay, asay usualay.
Eythay aidsay eirthay ayerspray, anday Idsay asway oonsay asleepay. Omtay aylay awakeay anday
aitedway, inay estlessray impatienceay. Enwhay itay eemedsay otay imhay atthay itay ustmay ebay
earlynay aylightday, ehay eardhay ethay ockclay ikestray entay! Isthay asway espairday. Ehay
ouldway avehay ossedtay anday idgetedfay, asay ishay ervesnay emandedday, utbay ehay asway
afraiday ehay ightmay akeway Idsay. Osay ehay aylay illstay, anday aredstay upay intoay ethay arkday.
Everythingay asway ismallyday illstay. Byay anday byay, outay ofay ethay illnessstay, ittlelay,
arcelyscay erceptiblepay oisesnay eganbay otay emphasizeay emselvesthay. Ethay ickingtay
ofay ethay ockclay eganbay otay ingbray itselfay intoay oticenay. Olday eamsbay eganbay otay ackcray
eriouslymystay. Ethay airsstay eakedcray aintlyfay. Evidentlyay iritsspay ereway abroaday.
Aay easuredmay, uffledmay oresnay issueday omfray Auntay Olly’spay amberchay. Anday ownay ethay
iresometay irpingchay ofay aay icketcray atthay onay umanhay ingenuityay ouldcay ocatelay,
eganbay. Extnay ethay astlyghay ickingtay ofay aay eath-watchday inay ethay allway atay ethay
ed’sbay eadhay ademay Omtay udder—itshay eantmay atthay omebody’ssay aysday ereway umberednay.
Enthay ethay owlhay ofay aay ar-offfay ogday oseray onay ethay ightnay airay, anday asway answereday
byay aay ainterfay owlhay omfray aay emoterray istanceday. Omtay asway inay anay agonyay. Atay astlay
ehay asway atisfiedsay atthay imetay adhay easedcay anday eternityay egunbay; ehay eganbay otay
ozeday, inay itespay ofay imselfhay; ethay ockclay imedchay elevenay, utbay ehay idday otnay earhay
itay. Anday enthay erethay amecay, inglingmay ithway ishay alf-formedhay eamsdray, aay ostmay
elancholymay aterwaulingcay. Ethay aisingray ofay aay eighboringnay indowway isturbedday
imhay. Aay cryay ofay at“scay! ouyay evil”day! anday ethay ashcray ofay anay emptyay ottlebay
againstay ethay ackbay ofay ishay aunt’say oodshedway oughtbray imhay ideway awakeay, anday aay
inglesay inutemay aterlay ehay asway esseddray anday outay ofay ethay indowway anday eepingcray
alongay ethay oofray ofay ethay ell”“ay onay allay oursfay. Ehay eow’d”“may ithway autioncay onceay
oray icetway, asay ehay entway; enthay umpedjay otay ethay oofray ofay ethay oodshedway anday encethay
otay ethay oundgray. Uckleberryhay Innfay asway erethay, ithway ishay eadday atcay. Ethay oysbay
ovedmay offay anday isappearedday inay ethay oomglay. Atay ethay enday ofay alfhay anay ourhay eythay
ereway adingway oughthray ethay alltay assgray ofay ethay aveyardgray.

Itay asway aay aveyardgray ofay ethay old-fashioneday Esternway indkay. Itay asway onay aay illhay,
aboutay aay ilemay anday aay alfhay omfray ethay illagevay. Itay adhay aay azycray oardbay encefay
arounday itay, ichwhay eanedlay inwarday inay acesplay, anday outwarday ethay estray ofay ethay
imetay, utbay oodstay uprightay owherenay. Assgray anday eedsway ewgray ankray overay ethay
olewhay emeterycay. Allay ethay olday avesgray ereway unkensay inay, erethay asway otnay aay
ombstonetay onay ethay aceplay; ound-toppedray, orm-eatenway oardsbay aggeredstay overay
ethay avesgray, eaninglay orfay upportsay anday indingfay onenay. acred“say otay ethay emorymay
of”ay O-and-Sosay adhay eenbay aintedpay onay emthay onceay, utbay itay ouldcay onay ongerlay avehay
eenbay eadray, onay ethay ostmay ofay emthay, ownay, evenay ifay erethay adhay eenbay ightlay.

Aay aintfay indway oanedmay oughthray ethay eestray, anday Omtay earedfay itay ightmay ebay ethay
iritsspay ofay ethay eadday, omplainingcay atay eingbay isturbedday. Ethay oysbay alkedtay
ittlelay, anday onlyay underay eirthay eathbray, orfay ethay imetay anday ethay aceplay anday ethay
ervadingpay olemnitysay anday ilencesay oppresseday eirthay iritsspay. Eythay oundfay ethay
arpshay ewnay eaphay eythay ereway eekingsay, anday ensconceday emselvesthay ithinway ethay
otectionpray ofay eethray eatgray elmsay atthay ewgray inay aay unchbay ithinway aay ewfay eetfay ofay
ethay avegray.

Ethay otway oysbay ewflay onay anday onay, owardtay ethay illagevay, eechlessspay ithway

atthay artedstay upay inay eirthay athpay eemedsay aay anmay anday anay enemyay, anday ademay emthay
atchcay eirthay eathbray; anday asay eythay edspay byay omesay outlyingay ottagescay atthay aylay
earnay ethay illagevay, ethay arkingbay ofay ethay arouseday atch-dogsway eemedsay otay ivegay
ingsway otay eirthay eetfay.

APTERchay IIxay


Oneay ofay ethay easonsray whyay Om’stay indmay adhay ifteddray awayay omfray itsay ecretsay

ouldshay ieday! Erethay asway istractionday inay ethay oughtthay. Ehay onay ongerlay ooktay anay

erethay asway onay oyjay inay emthay anyay oremay. Ishay auntay asway oncernedcay. Eshay eganbay otay
tryay allay annermay ofay emediesray onay imhay. Eshay asway oneay ofay osethay eoplepay owhay
areay infatuateday ithway atentpay edicinesmay anday allay ew-fanglednay ethodsmay ofay
oducingpray ealthhay oray endingmay itay. Eshay asway anay inveterateay experimenteray inay
esethay ingsthay. Enwhay omethingsay eshfray inay isthay inelay amecay outay eshay asway inay aay
everfay, ightray awayay, otay tryay itay; otnay onay erselfhay, orfay eshay asway evernay ailingay,
utbay onay anybodyay elseay atthay amecay andyhay. Eshay asway aay ubscribersay orfay allay ethay
ealth”“hay eriodicalspay anday enologicalphray audsfray; anday ethay olemnsay ignoranceay

APTERchay IIIxay


Om’stay indmay asway ademay upay ownay. Ehay asway oomyglay anday esperateday. Ehay asway aay
orsakenfay, iendlessfray oybay, ehay aidsay; obodynay ovedlay imhay; enwhay eythay oundfay outay

iendlessfray otay omplaincay? Esyay, eythay adhay orcedfay imhay otay itay atay astlay: ehay ouldway
eadlay aay ifelay ofay imecray. Erethay asway onay oicechay.

Byay isthay imetay ehay asway arfay ownday Eadowmay Anelay, anday ethay ellbay orfay oolschay otay

ardhay, utbay itay asway orcedfay onay imhay; incesay ehay asway ivendray outay intoay ethay oldcay
orldway, ehay ustmay ubmit—butsay ehay orgavefay emthay. Enthay ethay obssay amecay ickthay anday
astfay.

Ustjay atay isthay ointpay ehay etmay ishay oul’ssay ornsway omradecay, Oejay

atthay Oejay ouldway otnay orgetfay imhay.

Utbay itay anspiredtray atthay isthay asway aay equestray ichwhay Oejay adhay ustjay eenbay oinggay

oorpay oybay outay intoay ethay unfeelingay orldway otay uffersay anday ieday.

Eethray ilesmay elowbay Stay. Etersburgpay, atay aay ointpay erewhay ethay Ississippimay Iverray

Islanday asway osenchay. Owhay ereway otay ebay ethay ubjectssay ofay eirthay iraciespay asway aay

APTERchay IVxay


Enwhay Omtay awokeay inay ethay orningmay, ehay onderedway erewhay ehay asway. Ehay atsay upay anday
ubbedray ishay eyesay anday ookedlay arounday. Enthay ehay omprehendedcay. Itay asway ethay oolcay
aygray awnday, anday erethay asway aay eliciousday ensesay ofay eposeray anday eacepay inay ethay
eepday ervadingpay almcay anday ilencesay ofay ethay oodsway. Otnay aay eaflay irredstay; otnay
aay oundsay obtrudeday uponay eatgray Ature’snay editationmay. Eadedbay ewdropsday oodstay
uponay ethay eaveslay anday assesgray. Aay itewhay ayerlay ofay ashesay overedcay ethay irefay,
anday aay inthay ueblay eathbray ofay okesmay oseray aightstray intoay ethay airay. Oejay anday Uckhay
illstay eptslay.

Ownay, arfay awayay inay ethay oodsway aay irdbay alledcay; anotheray answereday; esentlypray
ethay ammeringhay ofay aay oodpeckerway asway eardhay. Aduallygray ethay oolcay imday aygray
ofay ethay orningmay itenedwhay, anday asay aduallygray oundssay ultipliedmay anday ifelay
anifestedmay itselfay. Ethay arvelmay ofay Aturenay akingshay offay eepslay anday oinggay
otay orkway unfoldeday itselfay otay ethay usingmay oybay. Aay ittlelay eengray ormway amecay
awlingcray overay aay ewyday eaflay, iftinglay o-thirdstway ofay ishay odybay intoay ethay airay
omfray imetay otay imetay anday iffing“snay around”ay, enthay oceedingpray again—foray ehay
asway easuringmay, Omtay aidsay; anday enwhay ethay ormway approacheday imhay, ofay itsay ownay
accorday, ehay atsay asay illstay asay aay onestay, ithway ishay opeshay isingray anday allingfay,
byay urnstay, asay ethay eaturecray illstay amecay owardtay imhay oray eemedsay inclineday otay
ogay elsewhereay; anday enwhay atay astlay itay onsideredcay aay ainfulpay omentmay ithway itsay
urvedcay odybay inay ethay airay anday enthay amecay ecisivelyday ownday uponay Om’stay eglay anday
eganbay aay ourneyjay overay imhay, ishay olewhay earthay asway ad—forglay atthay eantmay atthay
ehay asway oinggay otay avehay aay ewnay uitsay ofay othes—withoutclay ethay adowshay ofay aay
oubtday aay audygay iraticalpay uniformay. Ownay aay ocessionpray ofay antsay appeareday,
omfray owherenay inay articularpay, anday entway aboutay eirthay aborslay; oneay uggledstray
anfullymay byay ithway aay eadday iderspay ivefay imestay asay igbay asay itselfay inay itsay armsay,
anday uggedlay itay aightstray upay aay ee-trunktray. Aay ownbray ottedspay ady-buglay imbedclay
ethay izzyday eighthay ofay aay assgray adeblay, anday Omtay entbay ownday oseclay otay itay anday
aidsay, ady-bug“lay, ady-buglay, flyay awayay omehay, ouryay ousehay isay onay irefay, ouryay
ildren’schay alone”ay, anday eshay ooktay ingway anday entway offay otay eesay aboutay it—whichay
idday otnay urprisesay ethay oybay, orfay ehay ewknay ofay olday atthay isthay insectay asway
edulouscray aboutay onflagrationscay, anday ehay adhay actisedpray uponay itsay implicitysay
oremay anthay onceay. Aay umblebugtay amecay extnay, eavinghay urdilystay atay itsay allbay, anday
Omtay ouchedtay ethay eaturecray, otay eesay itay utshay itsay egslay againstay itsay odybay
anday etendpray otay ebay eadday. Ethay irdsbay ereway airlyfay iotingray byay isthay imetay. Aay
atbirdcay, ethay Orthernnay ockermay, itlay inay aay eetray overay Om’stay eadhay, anday illedtray
outay erhay imitationsay ofay erhay eighborsnay inay aay aptureray ofay enjoymentay; enthay
aay illshray ayjay eptsway ownday, aay ashflay ofay ueblay ameflay, anday oppedstay onay aay igtway
almostay ithinway ethay oy’sbay eachray, ockedcay ishay eadhay otay oneay idesay anday eyeday ethay
angersstray ithway aay onsumingcay uriositycay; aay aygray uirrelsqay anday aay igbay ellowfay
ofay ethay ox”“fay indkay amecay urryingskay alongay, ittingsay upay atay intervalsay otay
inspectay anday atterchay atay ethay oysbay, orfay ethay ildway ingsthay adhay obablypray evernay
eensay aay umanhay eingbay eforebay anday arcelyscay ewknay etherwhay otay ebay afraiday oray otnay.
Allay Aturenay asway ideway awakeay anday irringstay, ownay; onglay anceslay ofay unlightsay
iercedpay ownday oughthray ethay enseday oliagefay arfay anday earnay, anday aay ewfay
utterfliesbay amecay utteringflay uponay ethay enescay.

Omtay irredstay upay ethay otheray iratespay anday eythay allay atteredclay awayay ithway
aay outshay, anday inay aay inutemay oray otway ereway ippedstray anday asingchay afteray anday
umblingtay overay eachay otheray inay ethay allowshay impidlay aterway ofay ethay itewhay
andbarsay. Eythay eltfay onay onginglay orfay ethay ittlelay illagevay eepingslay inay ethay
istanceday eyondbay ethay ajesticmay asteway ofay aterway. Aay agrantvay urrentcay oray aay

atifiedgray emthay, incesay itsay oinggay asway omethingsay ikelay urningbay ethay idgebray
etweenbay emthay anday ivilizationcay.

Eythay amecay ackbay otay ampcay onderfullyway efreshedray, ad-heartedglay, anday
avenousray; anday eythay oonsay adhay ethay amp-firecay azingblay upay againay. Uckhay oundfay aay

oray ickoryhay eaveslay, anday eltfay atthay aterway, eetenedsway ithway uchsay aay ildwoodway
armchay asay atthay, ouldway ebay aay oodgay enoughay ubstitutesay orfay offeecay. Ilewhay Oejay
asway icingslay aconbay orfay eakfastbray, Omtay anday Uckhay askeday imhay otay oldhay onay aay
inutemay; eythay eppedstay otay aay omisingpray ooknay inay ethay iver-bankray anday ewthray inay

amilyfay. Eythay iedfray ethay ishfay ithway ethay aconbay, anday ereway astonisheday; orfay
onay ishfay adhay everay eemedsay osay eliciousday eforebay. Eythay idday otnay owknay atthay ethay
uickerqay aay esh-waterfray ishfay isay onay ethay irefay afteray ehay isay aughtcay ethay etterbay
ehay isay; anday eythay eflectedray ittlelay uponay atwhay aay aucesay open-airay eepingslay,
open-airay exerciseay, athingbay, anday aay argelay ingredientay ofay ungerhay akemay, ootay.

Eythay aylay arounday inay ethay adeshay, afteray eakfastbray, ilewhay Uckhay adhay aay okesmay,
anday enthay entway offay oughthray ethay oodsway onay anay exploringay expeditionay. Eythay
ampedtray aylygay alongay, overay ecayingday ogslay, oughthray angledtay underbrushay,
amongay olemnsay onarchsmay ofay ethay orestfay, unghay omfray eirthay ownscray otay ethay
oundgray ithway aay oopingdray egaliaray ofay ape-vinesgray. Ownay anday enthay eythay amecay
uponay ugsnay ooksnay arpetedcay ithway assgray anday eweledjay ithway owersflay.

Eythay oundfay entyplay ofay ingsthay otay ebay elightedday ithway, utbay othingnay otay ebay
astonisheday atay. Eythay iscoveredday atthay ethay islanday asway aboutay eethray ilesmay
onglay anday aay uarterqay ofay aay ilemay ideway, anday atthay ethay oreshay itay aylay osestclay otay
asway onlyay eparatedsay omfray itay byay aay arrownay annelchay ardlyhay otway undredhay ardsyay
ideway. Eythay ooktay aay imsway aboutay everyay ourhay, osay itay asway oseclay uponay ethay iddlemay
ofay ethay afternoonay enwhay eythay otgay ackbay otay ampcay. Eythay ereway ootay ungryhay otay
opstay otay ishfay, utbay eythay aredfay umptuouslysay uponay oldcay amhay, anday enthay ewthray
emselvesthay ownday inay ethay adeshay otay alktay. Utbay ethay alktay oonsay eganbay otay agdray,
anday enthay iedday. Ethay illnessstay, ethay olemnitysay atthay oodedbray inay ethay oodsway,
anday ethay ensesay ofay onelinesslay, eganbay otay elltay uponay ethay iritsspay ofay ethay oysbay.
Eythay ellfay otay inkingthay. Aay ortsay ofay undefineday onginglay eptcray uponay emthay. Isthay
ooktay imday apeshay, esently—itpray asway uddingbay omesicknesshay. Evenay Innfay ethay
Ed-Handedray asway eamingdray ofay ishay oorstepsday anday emptyay ogsheadshay. Utbay eythay
ereway allay ashameday ofay eirthay eaknessway, anday onenay asway avebray enoughay otay eakspay
ishay oughtthay.

Orfay omesay imetay, ownay, ethay oysbay adhay eenbay ullyday onsciouscay ofay aay eculiarpay
oundsay inay ethay istanceday, ustjay asay oneay ometimessay isay ofay ethay ickingtay ofay aay
ockclay ichwhay ehay akestay onay istinctday otenay ofay. Utbay ownay isthay eriousmystay oundsay
ecamebay oremay onouncedpray, anday orcedfay aay ecognitionray. Ethay oysbay artedstay,
ancedglay atay eachay otheray, anday enthay eachay assumeday aay isteninglay attitudeay. Erethay
asway aay onglay ilencesay, ofoundpray anday unbrokenay; enthay aay eepday, ullensay oombay amecay

Eythay angspray otay eirthay eetfay anday urriedhay otay ethay oreshay owardtay ethay owntay. Eythay

eamstay erry-boatfay asway aboutay aay ilemay elowbay ethay illagevay, iftingdray ithway ethay

anymay iffsskay owingray aboutay oray oatingflay ithway ethay eamstray inay ethay eighborhoodnay
ofay ethay erryboatfay, utbay ethay oysbay ouldcay otnay etermineday atwhay ethay enmay inay

erryboat’sfay idesay, anday asay itay expandeday anday oseray inay aay azylay oudclay, atthay amesay

at’s“thay it”ay! aidsay Uckhay; ey“thay oneday atthay astlay ummersay, enwhay Illbay Urnertay

APTERchay XVay


Aay ewfay inutesmay aterlay Omtay asway inay ethay oalshay aterway ofay ethay arbay, adingway owardtay
ethay Illinoisay oreshay. Eforebay ethay epthday eachedray ishay iddlemay ehay asway alfwayhay
overay; ethay urrentcay ouldway ermitpay onay oremay adingway, ownay, osay ehay uckstray outay
onfidentlycay otay imsway ethay emainingray undredhay ardsyay. Ehay amsway uarteringqay
upstreamay, utbay illstay asway eptsway ownwardday atherray asterfay anthay ehay adhay
expecteday. Oweverhay, ehay eachedray ethay oreshay inallyfay, anday ifteddray alongay illtay
ehay oundfay aay owlay aceplay anday ewdray imselfhay outay. Ehay utpay ishay andhay onay ishay acketjay
ocketpay, oundfay ishay iecepay ofay arkbay afesay, anday enthay uckstray oughthray ethay oodsway,
ollowingfay ethay oreshay, ithway eamingstray armentsgay. Ortlyshay eforebay entay

erryboatfay inglyay inay ethay adowshay ofay ethay eestray anday ethay ighhay ankbay. Everythingay

ithway allay ishay eyesay, ippedslay intoay ethay aterway, amsway eethray oray ourfay okesstray

aidlay imselfhay ownday underay ethay artsthway anday aitedway, antingpay.

Esentlypray ethay ackedcray ellbay appedtay anday aay oicevay avegay ethay orderay otay ast“cay

againstay ethay oat’sbay ellsway, anday ethay oyagevay asway egunbay. Omtay eltfay appyhay inay
ishay uccesssay, orfay ehay ewknay itay asway ethay oat’sbay astlay iptray orfay ethay ightnay. Atay
ethay enday ofay aay onglay elvetway oray ifteenfay inutesmay ethay eelswhay oppedstay, anday
Omtay ippedslay overboarday anday amsway ashoreay inay ethay uskday, andinglay iftyfay ardsyay
ownstreamday, outay ofay angerday ofay ossiblepay agglersstray.

ehay essedpray entlygay anday ethay oorday ieldedyay aay ackcray; ehay ontinuedcay ushingpay
autiouslycay, anday uakingqay everyay imetay itay eakedcray, illtay ehay udgedjay ehay ightmay
ueezesqay oughthray onay ishay eesknay; osay ehay utpay ishay eadhay oughthray anday eganbay,
arilyway.

at“whay akesmay ethay andlecay owblay o”say? aidsay Auntay Ollypay. Omtay urriedhay upay. “Whyay,

Mrsay. Arperhay avegay aay obbingsay oodnightgay anday urnedtay otay ogay. Enthay ithway aay

uffledsnay aay itbay anday Arymay entway offay ingcryay ithway allay erhay earthay.

Auntay Ollypay eltknay ownday anday ayedpray orfay Omtay osay ouchinglytay, osay appealinglyay,
anday ithway uchsay easurelessmay ovelay inay erhay ordsway anday erhay olday emblingtray oicevay,
atthay ehay asway elteringway inay earstay againay, onglay eforebay eshay asway oughthray.

Ehay adhay otay eepkay illstay onglay afteray eshay entway otay edbay, orfay eshay eptkay akingmay
oken-heartedbray ejaculationsay omfray imetay otay imetay, ossingtay unrestfullyay, anday

andle-lightcay ithway ishay andhay, anday oodstay egardingray erhay. Ishay earthay asway ullfay

andlecay. Utbay omethingsay occurreday otay imhay, anday ehay ingeredlay onsideringcay.
Ishay acefay ightedlay ithway aay appyhay olutionsay ofay ishay oughtthay; ehay utpay ethay arkbay
astilyhay inay ishay ocketpay. Enthay ehay entbay overay anday issedkay ethay adedfay ipslay, anday
aightwaystray ademay ishay ealthystay exitay, atchinglay ethay oorday ehindbay imhay.

Ehay eadedthray ishay ayway ackbay otay ethay erryfay andinglay, oundfay obodynay atay argelay

enantlesstay exceptay atthay erethay asway aay atchmanway, owhay alwaysay urnedtay inay anday
eptslay ikelay aay avengray imageay. Ehay untieday ethay iffskay atay ethay ernstay, ippedslay

APTERchay Ixvay


Afteray innerday allay ethay anggay urnedtay outay otay unthay orfay urtletay eggsay onay ethay arbay.
Eythay entway aboutay okingpay icksstay intoay ethay andsay, anday enwhay eythay oundfay aay oftsay
aceplay eythay entway ownday onay eirthay eesknay anday ugday ithway eirthay andshay. Ometimessay
eythay ouldway aketay iftyfay oray ixtysay eggsay outay ofay oneay olehay. Eythay ereway erfectlypay
oundray itewhay ingsthay aay ifletray allersmay anthay anay Englishay alnutway. Eythay adhay aay
amousfay ied-eggfray eastfay atthay ightnay, anday anotheray onay Idayfray orningmay.

Afteray eakfastbray eythay entway oopingwhay anday ancingpray outay onay ethay arbay, anday
asedchay eachay otheray oundray anday oundray, eddingshay othesclay asay eythay entway, untilay
eythay ereway akednay, anday enthay ontinuedcay ethay olicfray arfay awayay upay ethay oalshay
aterway ofay ethay arbay, againstay ethay iffstay urrentcay, ichwhay atterlay ippedtray eirthay
egslay omfray underay emthay omfray imetay otay imetay anday eatlygray increaseday ethay unfay.
Anday ownay anday enthay eythay oopedstay inay aay oupgray anday ashedsplay aterway inay eachay
other’say acesfay ithway eirthay almspay, aduallygray approachingay eachay otheray, ithway
averteday acesfay otay avoiday ethay anglingstray aysspray, anday inallyfay ippinggray anday
ugglingstray illtay ethay estbay anmay uckedday ishay eighbornay, anday enthay eythay allay
entway underay inay aay angletay ofay itewhay egslay anday armsay anday amecay upay owingblay,
utteringspay, aughinglay, anday aspinggay orfay eathbray atay oneay anday ethay amesay imetay.

Enwhay eythay ereway ellway exhausteday, eythay ouldway unray outay anday awlspray onay ethay dryay,
othay andsay, anday ielay erethay anday overcay emselvesthay upay ithway itay, anday byay anday byay
eakbray orfay ethay aterway againay anday ogay oughthray ethay originalay erformancepay onceay
oremay. Inallyfay itay occurreday otay emthay atthay eirthay akednay inskay epresentedray
esh-coloredflay ights”“tay eryvay airlyfay; osay eythay ewdray aay ingray inay ethay andsay anday
adhay aay ircus—withcay eethray ownsclay inay itay, orfay onenay ouldway ieldyay isthay oudestpray
ostpay otay ishay eighbornay.

Asay ethay unsay eganbay otay ealstay inay uponay ethay oysbay, owsinessdray amecay overay

ehay ouldcay. Utbay eythay aredcay othingnay orfay arblesmay, oray ircuscay, oray immingsway, oray
anythingay. Ehay emindedray emthay ofay ethay imposingay ecretsay, anday aisedray aay ayray ofay
eerchay. Ilewhay itay astedlay, ehay otgay emthay interesteday inay aay ewnay eviceday. Isthay asway
otay ockknay offay eingbay iratespay, orfay aay ilewhay, anday ebay Indiansay orfay aay angechay.

ippedstray, anday ipedstray omfray eadhay otay eelhay ithway ackblay udmay, ikelay osay anymay
ebras—allzay ofay emthay iefschay, ofay ourse—andcay enthay eythay entway earingtay oughthray
ethay oodsway otay attackay anay Englishay ettlementsay.

Byay anday byay eythay eparatedsay intoay eethray ostilehay ibestray, anday artedday uponay eachay
otheray omfray ambushay ithway eadfuldray arwhoopsway, anday illedkay anday alpedscay eachay
otheray byay ousandsthay. Itay asway aay orygay ayday. Onsequentlycay itay asway anay extremelyay
atisfactorysay oneay.

Eythay assembleday inay ampcay owardtay uppertimesay, ungryhay anday appyhay; utbay ownay
aay ifficultyday arose—hostileay Indiansay ouldcay otnay eakbray ethay eadbray ofay
ospitalityhay ogethertay ithoutway irstfay akingmay eacepay, anday isthay asway aay implesay
impossibilityay ithoutway okingsmay aay ipepay ofay eacepay. Erethay asway onay otheray
ocesspray atthay everay eythay adhay eardhay ofay. Otway ofay ethay avagessay almostay ishedway
eythay adhay emainedray iratespay. Oweverhay, erethay asway onay otheray ayway; osay ithway uchsay
owshay ofay eerfulnesschay asay eythay ouldcay ustermay eythay alledcay orfay ethay ipepay anday
ooktay eirthay iffwhay asay itay assedpay, inay ueday ormfay.

Anday eholdbay, eythay ereway adglay eythay adhay onegay intoay avagerysay, orfay eythay adhay
ainedgay omethingsay; eythay oundfay atthay eythay ouldcay ownay okesmay aay ittlelay ithoutway
avinghay otay ogay anday unthay orfay aay ostlay ifeknay; eythay idday otnay etgay icksay enoughay otay
ebay eriouslysay uncomfortableay. Eythay ereway otnay ikelylay otay oolfay awayay isthay ighhay
omisepray orfay acklay ofay effortay. Onay, eythay actisedpray autiouslycay, afteray uppersay,
ithway ightray airfay uccesssay, anday osay eythay entspay aay ubilantjay eveningay. Eythay ereway
ouderpray anday appierhay inay eirthay ewnay acquirementay anthay eythay ouldway avehay eenbay
inay ethay alpingscay anday inningskay ofay ethay Ixsay Ationsnay. Eway illway eavelay emthay otay
okesmay anday atterchay anday agbray, incesay eway avehay onay urtherfay useay orfay emthay atay
esentpray.




APTERchay IIxvay

ousehay. Itay asway isthay: etty“pray in—asthay onglay aay eamdray asay atthay, ithoutway anyay
istakesmay inay it”ay!

Atwhay aay erohay Omtay asway ecomebay, ownay! Ehay idday otnay ogay ippingskay anday ancingpray,
utbay ovedmay ithway aay ignifiedday aggersway asay ecamebay aay iratepay owhay eltfay atthay ethay
ublicpay eyeay asway onay imhay. Anday indeeday itay asway; ehay iedtray otnay otay eemsay otay eesay
ethay ookslay oray earhay ethay emarksray asay ehay assedpay alongay, utbay eythay ereway oodfay anday
inkdray otay imhay. Allersmay oysbay anthay imselfhay ockedflay atay ishay eelshay, asay oudpray
otay ebay eensay ithway imhay, anday oleratedtay byay imhay, asay ifay ehay adhay eenbay ethay ummerdray
atay ethay eadhay ofay aay ocessionpray oray ethay elephantay eadinglay aay enageriemay intoay
owntay. Oysbay ofay ishay ownay izesay etendedpray otnay otay owknay ehay adhay eenbay awayay atay
allay; utbay eythay ereway onsumingcay ithway envyay, everthelessnay. Eythay ouldway avehay
ivengay anythingay otay avehay atthay arthysway un-tannedsay inskay ofay ishay, anday ishay
itteringglay otorietynay; anday Omtay ouldway otnay avehay artedpay ithway eitheray orfay aay
ircuscay.

Atay oolschay ethay ildrenchay ademay osay uchmay ofay imhay anday ofay Oejay, anday eliveredday
uchsay eloquentay admirationay omfray eirthay eyesay, atthay ethay otway eroeshay ereway
otnay onglay inay ecomingbay insufferablyay uck-up”“stay. Eythay eganbay otay elltay eirthay
adventuresay otay ungryhay isteners—butlay eythay onlyay eganbay; itay asway otnay aay
ingthay ikelylay otay avehay anay enday, ithway imaginationsay ikelay eirsthay otay urnishfay
aterialmay. Anday inallyfay, enwhay eythay otgay outay eirthay ipespay anday entway erenelysay
uffingpay arounday, ethay eryvay ummitsay ofay oryglay asway eachedray.

Omtay ecidedday atthay ehay ouldcay ebay independentay ofay Eckybay Atcherthay ownay. Oryglay
asway ufficientsay. Ehay ouldway ivelay orfay oryglay. Ownay atthay ehay asway istinguishedday,
aybemay eshay ouldway ebay antingway otay ake“may up”ay. Ellway, etlay er—shehay ouldshay eesay
atthay ehay ouldcay ebay asay indifferentay asay omesay otheray eoplepay. Esentlypray eshay
arriveday. Omtay etendedpray otnay otay eesay erhay. Ehay ovedmay awayay anday oinedjay aay oupgray
ofay oysbay anday irlsgay anday eganbay otay alktay. Oonsay ehay observeday atthay eshay asway
ippingtray aylygay ackbay anday orthfay ithway ushedflay acefay anday ancingday eyesay,
etendingpray otay ebay usybay asingchay oolmatesschay, anday eamingscray ithway aughterlay
enwhay eshay ademay aay apturecay; utbay ehay oticednay atthay eshay alwaysay ademay erhay
apturescay inay ishay icinityvay, anday atthay eshay eemedsay otay astcay aay onsciouscay eyeay
inay ishay irectionday atay uchsay imestay, ootay. Itay atifiedgray allay ethay iciousvay anityvay
atthay asway inay imhay; anday osay, insteaday ofay inningway imhay, itay onlyay et“say imhay up”ay
ethay oremay anday ademay imhay ethay oremay iligentday otay avoiday etrayingbay atthay ehay
ewknay eshay asway aboutay. Esentlypray eshay avegay overay arkingskylay, anday ovedmay
irresolutelyay aboutay, ighingsay onceay oray icetway anday ancingglay urtivelyfay anday
istfullyway owardtay Omtay. Enthay eshay observeday atthay ownay Omtay asway alkingtay oremay
articularlypay otay Amyay Awrencelay anthay otay anyay oneay elseay. Eshay eltfay aay arpshay angpay
anday ewgray isturbedday anday uneasyay atay onceay. Eshay iedtray otay ogay awayay, utbay erhay
eetfay ereway eacheroustray, anday arriedcay erhay otay ethay oupgray insteaday. Eshay aidsay otay
aay irlgay almostay atay Om’stay elbow—withay amshay ivacityvay:

“Whyay, Arymay Austinay! ouyay adbay irlgay, whyay idn’tday ouyay omecay otay Unday-school”say?

I“ay idday ome—didn’tcay ouyay eesay e”may?

id“day ouyay? Whyay, it’say unnyfay Iay idn’tday eesay ouyay. Iay antedway otay elltay ouyay aboutay
ethay icnic”pay.

Anday osay onay, ithway appingclay ofay oyfuljay andshay illtay allay ethay oupgray adhay eggedbay

alkingtay, anday ooktay Amyay ithway imhay. Ecky’sbay ipslay embledtray anday ethay earstay
amecay otay erhay eyesay; eshay idhay esethay ignssay ithway aay orcedfay ayetygay anday entway onay
atteringchay, utbay ethay ifelay adhay onegay outay ofay ethay icnicpay, ownay, anday outay ofay

elf-satisfactionsay. Anday ehay eptkay iftingdray aboutay otay indfay Eckybay anday aceratelay

ethay oolhouseschay ookinglay atay aay icture-bookpay ithway Alfreday Emple—andtay osay

Ealousyjay anray ed-hotray oughthray Om’stay einsvay. Ehay eganbay otay atehay imselfhay orfay
owingthray awayay ethay ancechay Eckybay adhay offereday orfay aay econciliationray. Ehay

antedway otay cryay ithway exationvay. Amyay attedchay appilyhay alongay, asay eythay alkedway,

idday otnay earhay atwhay Amyay asway ayingsay, anday eneverwhay eshay ausedpay expectantlyay

againay, otay earsay ishay eyeballsay ithway ethay atefulhay ectaclespay erethay. Ehay ouldcay

ivinglay. Utbay eshay idday eesay, everthelessnay; anday eshay ewknay eshay asway inningway erhay
ightfay, ootay, anday asway adglay otay eesay imhay uffersay asay eshay adhay ufferedsay.

Amy’say appyhay attlepray ecamebay intolerableay. Omtay intedhay atay ingsthay ehay adhay

aidsay artlesslyay atthay eshay ouldway ebay around”“ay enwhay oolschay etlay outay. Anday ehay
astenedhay awayay, atinghay erhay orfay itay.

Any“ay otheray oy”bay! Omtay oughtthay, atinggray ishay eethtay. Any“ay oybay inay ethay olewhay
owntay utbay atthay Aintsay Ouislay artysmay atthay inksthay ehay essesdray osay inefay anday isay

Anday ehay entway oughthray ethay otionsmay ofay ashingthray anay imaginaryay oy—pummellingbay
ethay airay, anday ickingkay anday ouginggay. Oh“ay, ouyay oday, oday ouyay? Ouyay ollerhay
ough’nay, oday ouyay? Ownay, enthay, etlay atthay earnlay ou”yay! Anday osay ethay imaginaryay
oggingflay asway inishedfay otay ishay atisfactionsay.

Omtay edflay omehay atay oonnay. Ishay onsciencecay ouldcay otnay endureay anyay oremay ofay Amy’say

o“gay awayay anday eavelay emay aloneay, an’tcay ouyay! Iay atehay ou”yay!

Osay ethay oybay altedhay, onderingway atwhay ehay ouldcay avehay one—forday eshay adhay aidsay

accountay, anday otay atehay imhay oreverfay, intoay ethay argainbay.




APTERchay IXxay


Omtay arriveday atay omehay inay aay earydray oodmay, anday ethay irstfay ingthay ishay auntay aidsay

om“tay, I’veay aay otionnay otay inskay ouyay alive”ay!

Auntie“ay, atwhay avehay Iay one”day?

ell“way, ou’veyay oneday enoughay. Erehay Iay ogay overay otay Erenysay Arperhay, ikelay anay olday
oftysay, expectingay I’may oinggay otay akemay erhay elievebay allay atthay ubbageray aboutay
atthay eamdray, enwhay olay anday eholdbay ouyay e’dshay oundfay outay omfray Oejay atthay ouyay asway
overay erehay anday eardhay allay ethay alktay eway adhay atthay ightnay. Omtay, Iay on’tday owknay
atwhay isay otay ecomebay ofay aay oybay atthay illway actay ikelay atthay. Itay akesmay emay eelfay osay
adbay otay inkthay ouyay ouldcay etlay emay ogay otay Erenysay Arperhay anday akemay uchsay aay oolfay
ofay elfmysay anday evernay aysay aay ord”way.

Isthay asway aay ewnay aspectay ofay ethay ingthay. Ishay artnesssmay ofay ethay orningmay adhay

Ackson’sjay Islanday inay ethay ightnay otay aughlay atay ouray oublestray, anday ouyay ouldcay

orse”way.

ecause“bay Iay ovedlay ouyay osay, anday ouyay aidlay erethay oaningmay anday Iay asway osay orry”say.

iss“kay emay againay, Om—andtay! ebay offay ithway ouyay otay oolschay, ownay, anday on’tday

ielay. Iay on’tway ook”lay.

Eshay utpay ethay acketjay awayay, anday oodstay byay usingmay aay inutemay. Icetway eshay utpay outay

eshay enturedvay, anday isthay imetay eshay ortifiedfay erselfhay ithway ethay oughtthay:
It’s“ay aay oodgay ie—it’slay aay oodgay ie—Ilay on’tway etlay itay ievegray e”may. Osay eshay
oughtsay ethay acketjay ocketpay. Aay omentmay aterlay eshay asway eadingray Om’stay iecepay ofay
arkbay oughthray owingflay earstay anday ayingsay: I“ay ouldcay orgivefay ethay oybay, ownay, ifay
e’dhay ommittedcay aay illionmay ins”say!




APTERchay XXay


Erethay asway omethingsay aboutay Auntay Olly’spay annermay, enwhay eshay issedkay Omtay, atthay
eptsway awayay ishay owlay iritsspay anday ademay imhay ightheartedlay anday appyhay againay. Ehay
artedstay otay oolschay anday adhay ethay ucklay ofay omingcay uponay Eckybay Atcherthay atay ethay
eadhay ofay Eadowmay Anelay. Ishay oodmay alwaysay eterminedday ishay annermay. Ithoutway aay
oment’smay esitationhay ehay anray otay erhay anday aidsay:

I“ay acteday ightymay eanmay odaytay, Eckybay, anday I’may osay orrysay. Iay on’tway everay, everay
oday atthay ayway againay, asay onglay asay everay Iay ive—pleaselay akemay upay, on’tway ou”yay?

Ethay irlgay oppedstay anday ookedlay imhay ornfullyscay inay ethay acefay:

I’ll“ay ankthay ouyay otay eepkay ourselfyay o__tay ourselfyay, Mray. Omasthay Awyersay. I’llay
evernay eakspay otay ouyay again”ay.

Eshay ossedtay erhay eadhay anday assedpay onay. Omtay asway osay unnedstay atthay ehay adhay otnay
evenay esencepray ofay indmay enoughay otay aysay o“whay arescay, Issmay Arty”smay? untilay ethay
ightray imetay otay aysay itay adhay onegay byay. Osay ehay aidsay othingnay. Utbay ehay asway inay aay
inefay ageray, everthelessnay. Ehay opedmay intoay ethay oolyardschay ishingway eshay ereway
aay oybay, anday imaginingay owhay ehay ouldway ouncetray erhay ifay eshay ereway. Ehay esentlypray
encountereday erhay anday eliveredday aay ingingstay emarkray asay ehay assedpay. Eshay urledhay
oneay inay eturnray, anday ethay angryay eachbray asway ompletecay. Itay eemedsay otay Eckybay, inay
erhay othay esentmentray, atthay eshay ouldcay ardlyhay aitway orfay oolschay otay ake“tay in”ay,
eshay asway osay impatientay otay eesay Omtay oggedflay orfay ethay injureday elling-bookspay.
Ifay eshay adhay adhay anyay ingeringlay otionnay ofay exposingay Alfreday Empletay, Om’stay
offensiveay ingflay adhay ivendray itay entirelyay awayay.

Oorpay irlgay, eshay idday otnay owknay owhay astfay eshay asway earingnay oubletray erselfhay.
Ethay astermay, Mray. Obbinsday, adhay eachedray iddlemay ageay ithway anay unsatisfieday
ambitionay. Ethay arlingday ofay ishay esiresday asway, otay ebay aay octorday, utbay
overtypay adhay ecreedday atthay ehay ouldshay ebay othingnay igherhay anthay aay illagevay
oolmasterschay. Everyay ayday ehay ooktay aay eriousmystay ookbay outay ofay ishay eskday anday
absorbeday imselfhay inay itay atay imestay enwhay onay assesclay ereway ecitingray. Ehay eptkay
atthay ookbay underay ocklay anday eykay. Erethay asway otnay anay urchinay inay oolschay utbay asway
erishingpay otay avehay aay impseglay ofay itay, utbay ethay ancechay evernay amecay. Everyay oybay
anday irlgay adhay aay eorythay aboutay ethay aturenay ofay atthay ookbay; utbay onay otway eoriesthay
ereway alikeay, anday erethay asway onay ayway ofay ettinggay atay ethay actsfay inay ethay asecay.
Ownay, asay Eckybay asway assingpay byay ethay eskday, ichwhay oodstay earnay ethay oorday, eshay
oticednay atthay ethay eykay asway inay ethay ocklay! Itay asway aay eciouspray omentmay. Eshay
ancedglay arounday; oundfay erselfhay aloneay, anday ethay extnay instantay eshay adhay ethay
ookbay inay erhay andshay. Ethay itlepage—Professortay Omebody’ssay Anatomy_—carried_ay
onay informationay otay erhay indmay; osay eshay eganbay otay urntay ethay eaveslay. Eshay amecay atay
onceay uponay aay andsomelyhay engraveday anday oloredcay ontispiece—afray umanhay igurefay,
arkstay akednay. Atay atthay omentmay aay adowshay ellfay onay ethay agepay anday Omtay Awyersay
eppedstay inay atay ethay oorday anday aughtcay aay impseglay ofay ethay icturepay. Eckybay
atchedsnay atay ethay ookbay otay oseclay itay, anday adhay ethay ardhay ucklay otay eartay ethay
icturedpay agepay alfhay ownday ethay iddlemay. Eshay ustthray ethay olumevay intoay ethay eskday,
urnedtay ethay eykay, anday urstbay outay ingcryay ithway ameshay anday exationvay.

ow“hay ouldcay Iay owknay ouyay asway ookinglay atay anything”ay?

Omtay otshay aay anceglay atay Eckybay. Ehay adhay eensay aay untedhay anday elplesshay abbitray

orfay Eckybay ownay, ehay aidsay. Ethay extnay omentmay ethay astermay acedfay ethay oolschay.

APTERchay Ixxay


Acationvay asway approachingay. Ethay oolmasterschay, alwaysay everesay, ewgray everersay
anday oremay exactingay anthay everay, orfay ehay antedway ethay oolschay otay akemay aay oodgay
owingshay onay Examination”“ay ayday. Ishay odray anday ishay erulefay ereway eldomsay idleay
ow—atnay eastlay amongay ethay allersmay upilspay. Onlyay ethay iggestbay oysbay, anday oungyay
adieslay ofay eighteenay anday entytway, escapeday ashinglay. Mray. Obbins’day ashingslay
ereway eryvay igorousvay onesay, ootay; orfay althoughay ehay arriedcay, underay ishay igway, aay
erfectlypay aldbay anday inyshay eadhay, ehay adhay onlyay eachedray iddlemay ageay, anday erethay
asway onay ignsay ofay eeblenessfay inay ishay usclemay. Asay ethay eatgray ayday approacheday,
allay ethay annytyray atthay asway inay imhay amecay otay ethay urfacesay; ehay eemedsay otay aketay aay
indictivevay easureplay inay unishingpay ethay eastlay ortcomingsshay. Ethay onsequencecay
asway, atthay ethay allersmay oysbay entspay eirthay aysday inay errortay anday ufferingsay anday
eirthay ightsnay inay ottingplay evengeray. Eythay ewthray awayay onay opportunityay otay oday
ethay astermay aay ischiefmay. Utbay ehay eptkay aheaday allay ethay imetay. Ethay etributionray
atthay ollowedfay everyay engefulvay uccesssay asway osay eepingsway anday ajesticmay atthay
ethay oysbay alwaysay etiredray omfray ethay ieldfay adlybay orstedway. Atay astlay eythay
onspiredcay ogethertay anday ithay uponay aay anplay atthay omisedpray aay azzlingday ictoryvay.
Eythay oresway inay ethay ignpainter’ssay oybay, oldtay imhay ethay emeschay, anday askeday ishay
elphay. Ehay adhay ishay ownay easonsray orfay eingbay elightedday, orfay ethay astermay oardedbay
inay ishay ather’sfay amilyfay anday adhay ivengay ethay oybay ampleay ausecay otay atehay imhay.
Ethay aster’smay ifeway ouldway ogay onay aay isitvay otay ethay ountrycay inay aay ewfay aysday, anday
erethay ouldway ebay othingnay otay interfereay ithway ethay anplay; ethay astermay alwaysay
eparedpray imselfhay orfay eatgray occasionsay byay ettinggay ettypray ellway uddledfay, anday
ethay ignpainter’ssay oybay aidsay atthay enwhay ethay ominieday adhay eachedray ethay operpray
onditioncay onay Examinationay Eveningay ehay ouldway anage“may ethay ing”thay ilewhay ehay
appednay inay ishay airchay; enthay ehay ouldway avehay imhay awakeneday atay ethay ightray imetay
anday urriedhay awayay otay oolschay.

Inay ethay ulnessfay ofay imetay ethay interestingay occasionay arriveday. Atay eightay inay
ethay eveningay ethay oolhouseschay asway illiantlybray ightedlay, anday adorneday ithway
eathswray anday estoonsfay ofay oliagefay anday owersflay. Ethay astermay atsay onedthray inay
ishay eatgray airchay uponay aay aisedray atformplay, ithway ishay ackboardblay ehindbay imhay.
Ehay asway ookinglay olerablytay ellowmay. Eethray owsray ofay enchesbay onay eachay idesay anday
ixsay owsray inay ontfray ofay imhay ereway occupieday byay ethay ignitariesday ofay ethay owntay
anday byay ethay arentspay ofay ethay upilspay. Otay ishay eftlay, ackbay ofay ethay owsray ofay
itizenscay, asway aay aciousspay emporarytay atformplay uponay ichwhay ereway eatedsay ethay
olarsschay owhay ereway otay aketay artpay inay ethay exercisesay ofay ethay eveningay; owsray ofay
allsmay oysbay, ashedway anday esseddray otay anay intolerableay atestay ofay iscomfortday;
owsray ofay awkygay igbay oysbay; owbankssnay ofay irlsgay anday oungyay adieslay adclay inay
awnlay anday uslinmay anday onspicuouslycay onsciouscay ofay eirthay arebay armsay, eirthay
andmothers’gray ancientay inketstray, eirthay itsbay ofay inkpay anday ueblay ibbonray anday
ethay owersflay inay eirthay airhay. Allay ethay estray ofay ethay ousehay asway illedfay ithway
on-participatingnay olarsschay.

Ethay exercisesay eganbay. Aay eryvay ittlelay oybay oodstay upay anday eepishlyshay ecitedray,
ou’d“yay arcescay expectay oneay ofay myay ageay otay eakspay inay ublicpay onay ethay age”stay,
etc—accompanyingay. imselfhay ithway ethay ainfullypay exactay anday asmodicspay
esturesgay ichwhay aay achinemay ightmay avehay used—supposingay ethay achinemay otay ebay aay
ifletray outay ofay orderay. Utbay ehay otgay oughthray afelysay, oughthay uellycray aredscay,
anday otgay aay inefay oundray ofay applauseay enwhay ehay ademay ishay anufacturedmay owbay anday
etiredray.

Aay ittlelay amefacedshay irlgay ispedlay, ary“may adhay aay ittlelay amb”lay, etc,ay.
erformedpay aay ompassion-inspiringcay urtsycay, otgay erhay eedmay ofay applauseay, anday
atsay ownday ushedflay anday appyhay.

Omtay Awyersay eppedstay orwardfay ithway onceitedcay onfidencecay anday oaredsay intoay
ethay unquenchableay anday indestructibleay ive“gay emay ibertylay oray ivegay emay eath”day
eechspay, ithway inefay uryfay anday anticfray esticulationgay, anday okebray ownday inay ethay
iddlemay ofay itay. Aay astlyghay age-frightstay eizedsay imhay, ishay egslay uakedqay underay
imhay anday ehay asway ikelay otay okechay. Uetray, ehay adhay ethay anifestmay athysympay ofay ethay
ousehay utbay ehay adhay ethay ouse’shay ilencesay, ootay, ichwhay asway evenay orseway anthay
itsay athysympay. Ethay astermay ownedfray, anday isthay ompletedcay ethay isasterday. Omtay
uggledstray awhileay anday enthay etiredray, utterlyay efeatedday. Erethay asway aay eakway
attemptay atay applauseay, utbay itay iedday earlyay.

e“thay Oybay Oodstay onay ethay Urningbay Eck”day ollowedfay; alsoay e“thay Assyrianay Amecay
Own”day, anday otheray eclamatoryday emsgay. Enthay erethay ereway eadingray exercisesay,

imepray eaturefay ofay ethay eveningay asway inay orderay, ow—originalnay ompositions”“cay
byay ethay oungyay adieslay. Eachay inay erhay urntay eppedstay orwardfay otay ethay edgeay ofay ethay
atformplay, earedclay erhay oatthray, eldhay upay erhay anuscriptmay ied(tay ithway aintyday
ibbon)ray, anday oceededpray otay eadray, ithway aboredlay attentionay otay expression”“ay
anday unctuationpay. Ethay emesthay ereway ethay amesay atthay adhay eenbay illuminateday uponay
imilarsay occasionsay byay eirthay othersmay eforebay emthay, eirthay andmothersgray, anday
oubtlessday allay eirthay ancestorsay inay ethay emalefay inelay earclay ackbay otay ethay
Usadescray. iendship”“fray asway oneay; emories“may ofay Otheray Ays”day; eligion“ray inay
Istory”hay; eam“dray And”lay; e“thay Advantagesay ofay Ulture”cay; orms“fay ofay Oliticalpay
Overnmentgay Omparedcay anday Ontrasted”cay; elancholy”“may; ilial“fay Ove”lay; eart“hay
Ongings”lay, etc,ay. etcay.

Aay evalentpray eaturefay inay esethay ompositionscay asway aay ursednay anday ettedpay
elancholymay; anotheray asway aay astefulway anday opulentay ushgay ofay ine“fay anguage”lay;
anotheray asway aay endencytay otay uglay inay byay ethay earsay articularlypay izedpray ordsway
anday asesphray untilay eythay ereway ornway entirelyay outay; anday aay eculiaritypay atthay
onspicuouslycay arkedmay anday arredmay emthay asway ethay inveterateay anday intolerableay
ermonsay atthay aggedway itsay ippledcray ailtay atay ethay enday ofay eachay anday everyay oneay ofay
emthay. Onay attermay atwhay ethay ubjectsay ightmay ebay, aay ainrackingbray effortay asway
ademay otay uirmsqay itay intoay omesay aspectay oray otheray atthay ethay oralmay anday eligiousray
indmay ouldcay ontemplatecay ithway edificationay. Ethay aringglay insincerityay ofay
esethay ermonssay asway otnay ufficientsay otay ompasscay ethay anishmentbay ofay ethay
ashionfay omfray ethay oolsschay, anday itay isay otnay ufficientsay odaytay; itay evernay illway
ebay ufficientsay ilewhay ethay orldway andsstay, erhapspay. Erethay isay onay oolschay inay allay
ouray andlay erewhay ethay oungyay adieslay oday otnay eelfay obligeday otay oseclay eirthay

ostmay ivolousfray anday ethay eastlay eligiousray irlgay inay ethay oolschay isay alwaysay ethay
ongestlay anday ethay ostmay elentlesslyray iouspay. Utbay enoughay ofay isthay. Omelyhay
uthtray isay unpalatableay.

Etlay usay eturnray otay ethay Examination”“ay. Ethay irstfay ompositioncay atthay asway eadray
asway oneay entitleday Is“ay isthay, enthay, Ife”lay? Erhapspay ethay eaderray ancay endureay anay
extractay omfray itay:

In“ay ethay ommoncay alksway ofay ifelay, ithway atwhay elightfulday emotionsay oesday ethay
outhfulyay indmay ooklay orwardfay otay omesay anticipateday enescay ofay estivityfay!
Imaginationay isay usybay etchingskay ose-tintedray icturespay ofay oyjay. Inay ancyfay, ethay
oluptuousvay otaryvay ofay ashionfay eessay erselfhay amiday ethay estivefay ongthray, e‘thay
observeday ofay allay observers’ay. Erhay acefulgray ormfay, arrayeday inay owysnay obesray,
isay irlingwhay oughthray ethay azesmay ofay ethay oyousjay anceday; erhay eyeay isay ightestbray,
erhay epstay isay ightestlay inay ethay aygay assemblyay.

In“ay uchsay eliciousday anciesfay imetay uicklyqay idesglay byay, anday ethay elcomeway ourhay
arrivesay orfay erhay entranceay intoay ethay Elysianay orldway, ofay ichwhay eshay ashay
adhay uchsay ightbray eamsdray. Owhay airy-likefay oesday everythingay appearay otay erhay
enchanteday isionvay! Eachay ewnay enescay isay oremay armingchay anthay ethay astlay. Utbay
afteray aay ilewhay eshay indsfay atthay eneathbay isthay oodlygay exterioray, allay isay
anityvay, ethay atteryflay ichwhay onceay armedchay erhay oulsay, ownay atesgray arshlyhay
uponay erhay earay; ethay allroombay ashay ostlay itsay armschay; anday ithway astedway ealthhay
anday imbittereday earthay, eshay urnstay awayay ithway ethay onvictioncay atthay earthlyay
easuresplay annotcay atisfysay ethay ongingslay ofay ethay oul”say!

APTERchay IIxxay


Omtay oinedjay ethay ewnay orderay ofay Adetscay ofay Emperancetay, eingbay attracteday byay ethay
owyshay aracterchay ofay eirthay egalia”“ray. Ehay omisedpray otay abstainay omfray okingsmay,

Udgejay Azerfray, usticejay ofay ethay eacepay, owhay asway apparentlyay onay ishay eathbedday

ooking-glasslay. Utbay ethay Udgejay adhay aay ostmay iscouragingday ayway ofay uctuatingflay.
Atay astlay ehay asway onouncedpray uponay ethay end—andmay enthay onvalescentcay. Omtay asway
isgustedday; anday eltfay aay ensesay ofay injuryay, ootay. Ehay andedhay inay ishay esignationray
atay once—anday atthay ightnay ethay Udgejay ufferedsay aay elapseray anday iedday. Omtay
esolvedray atthay ehay ouldway evernay usttray aay anmay ikelay atthay againay.

ouldcay, ooktay ethay esireday awayay, anday ethay armchay ofay itay.

Omtay esentlypray onderedway otay indfay atthay ishay ovetedcay acationvay asway eginningbay
otay anghay aay ittlelay eavilyhay onay ishay andshay.

Ehay attempteday aay iary—butday othingnay appenedhay uringday eethray aysday, anday osay ehay
abandoneday itay.

Ethay irstfay ofay allay ethay egronay instrelmay owsshay amecay otay owntay, anday ademay aay

Uringday otway onglay eeksway Omtay aylay aay isonerpray, eadday otay ethay orldway anday itsay

Byay anday byay ethay empesttay entspay itselfay anday iedday ithoutway accomplishingay itsay

ishin’fay acesplay asway, anday efriendbay em’ay atwhay Iay ouldcay, anday ownay ey’vethay

on’t—_they_day on’tday orgetfay im’hay, ayssay Iay, and‘ay Iay on’tday orgetfay em’thay. Ellway,
oysbay, Iay oneday anay awfulay ing—drunkthay anday azycray atay ethay ime—that’stay ethay onlyay
ayway Iay accountay orfay it—anday ownay Iay otgay otay ingsway orfay itay, anday it’say ightray.
Ightray, anday est__bay, ootay, Iay eckon—hoperay osay, anywayay. Ellway, eway on’tway alktay
aboutay atthay. Iay on’tday antway otay akemay ou__yay eelfay adbay; ou’veyay efriendedbay emay.
Utbay atwhay Iay antway otay aysay, isay, on’tday ou__yay everay etgay unk—thendray ouyay on’tway
everay etgay erehay. Andstay aay itterlay urderfay est—so—that’sway itay; it’say aay imepray
omfortcay otay eesay acesfay at’sthay iendlyfray enwhay aay ody’sbay inay uchsay aay uckmay
ofay oubletray, anday erethay on’tday onenay omecay erehay utbay ournyay. Oodgay iendlyfray
aces—goodfay iendlyfray acesfay. Itgay upay onay oneay another’say acksbay anday etlay emay
ouchtay em’ay. At’sthay itay. Akeshay ands—yourn’llhay omecay oughthray ethay arsbay, utbay
ine’smay ootay igbay. Ittlelay andshay, anday eak—butway ey’vethay elpedhay Uffmay Otterpay aay
owerpay, anday ey’dthay elphay imhay oremay ifay eythay ould”cay.

Omtay entway omehay iserablemay, anday ishay eamsdray atthay ightnay ereway ullfay ofay orrorshay.
Ethay extnay ayday anday ethay ayday afteray, ehay unghay aboutay ethay ourtroomcay, awndray byay anay
almostay irresistibleay impulseay otay ogay inay, utbay orcingfay imselfhay otay aystay outay.
Uckhay asway avinghay ethay amesay experienceay. Eythay udiouslystay avoideday eachay otheray.
Eachay anderedway awayay, omfray imetay otay imetay, utbay ethay amesay ismalday ascinationfay
alwaysay oughtbray emthay ackbay esentlypray. Omtay eptkay ishay earsay openay enwhay idlersay
aunteredsay outay ofay ethay ourtroomcay, utbay invariablyay eardhay istressingday
ews—thenay oilstay ereway osingclay oremay anday oremay elentlesslyray arounday oorpay
Otterpay. Atay ethay enday ofay ethay econdsay ayday ethay illagevay alktay asway otay ethay effectay

otnay ethay ightestslay uestionqay asay otay atwhay ethay ury’sjay erdictvay ouldway ebay.

Omtay asway outay atelay, atthay ightnay, anday amecay otay edbay oughthray ethay indowway. Ehay
asway inay aay emendoustray atestay ofay excitementay. Itay asway ourshay eforebay ehay otgay otay
eepslay. Allay ethay illagevay ockedflay otay ethay ourthousecay ethay extnay orningmay, orfay

APTERchay IVxxay


Omtay asway aay itteringglay erohay onceay ore—themay etpay ofay ethay olday, ethay envyay ofay ethay
oungyay. Ishay amenay evenay entway intoay immortalay intpray, orfay ethay illagevay aperpay
agnifiedmay imhay. Erethay ereway omesay atthay elievedbay ehay ouldway ebay Esidentpray, etyay,
ifay ehay escapeday anginghay.

Asay usualay, ethay icklefay, unreasoningay orldway ooktay Uffmay Otterpay otay itsay osombay
anday ondledfay imhay asay avishlylay asay itay adhay abuseday imhay eforebay. Utbay atthay ortsay
ofay onductcay isay otay ethay orld’sway editcray; ereforethay itay isay otnay ellway otay indfay
aultfay ithway itay.

Om’stay aysday ereway aysday ofay endorsplay anday exultationay otay imhay, utbay ishay ightsnay
ereway easonssay ofay orrorhay. Injunay Oejay infesteday allay ishay eamsdray, anday alwaysay
ithway oomday inay ishay eyeay. Ardlyhay anyay emptationtay ouldcay ersuadepay ethay oybay
otay irstay abroaday afteray ightfallnay. Oorpay Uckhay asway inay ethay amesay atestay ofay
etchednesswray anday errortay, orfay Omtay adhay oldtay ethay olewhay orystay otay ethay awyerlay
ethay ightnay eforebay ethay eatgray ayday ofay ethay ialtray, anday Uckhay asway oresay afraiday
atthay ishay areshay inay ethay usinessbay ightmay eaklay outay, etyay, otwithstandingnay
Injunay Oe’sjay ightflay adhay avedsay imhay ethay ufferingsay ofay estifyingtay inay ourtcay.
Ethay oorpay ellowfay adhay otgay ethay attorneyay otay omisepray ecrecysay, utbay atwhay ofay
atthay? Incesay Om’stay arassedhay onsciencecay adhay anagedmay otay ivedray imhay otay ethay
awyer’slay ousehay byay ightnay anday ingwray aay eaddray aletay omfray ipslay atthay adhay
eenbay ealedsay ithway ethay ismalestday anday ostmay ormidablefay ofay oathsay, Uck’shay
onfidencecay inay ethay umanhay aceray asway ellnighway obliterateday.

Ailyday Uffmay Otter’spay atitudegray ademay Omtay adglay ehay adhay okenspay; utbay ightlynay
ehay ishedway ehay adhay ealedsay upay ishay onguetay.

Alfhay ethay imetay Omtay asway afraiday Injunay Oejay ouldway evernay ebay apturedcay; ethay
otheray alfhay ehay asway afraiday ehay ouldway ebay. Ehay eltfay uresay ehay evernay ouldcay awdray aay
afesay eathbray againay untilay atthay anmay asway eadday anday ehay adhay eensay ethay orpsecay.

Ewardsray adhay eenbay offereday, ethay ountrycay adhay eenbay ouredscay, utbay onay Injunay
Oejay asway oundfay. Oneay ofay osethay omniscientay anday awe-inspiringay arvelsmay, aay
etectiveday, amecay upay omfray Stay. Ouislay, ousedmay arounday, ookshay ishay eadhay, ookedlay
iseway, anday ademay atthay ortsay ofay astoundingay uccesssay ichwhay embersmay ofay atthay
aftcray usuallyay achieveay. Atthay isay otay aysay, ehay ound“fay aay ew”clay. Utbay ouyay an’tcay
anghay aay ew”“clay orfay urdermay, anday osay afteray atthay etectiveday adhay otgay oughthray
anday onegay omehay, Omtay eltfay ustjay asay insecureay asay ehay asway eforebay.

Ethay owslay aysday ifteddray onay, anday eachay eftlay ehindbay itay aay ightlyslay ightenedlay
eightway ofay apprehensionay.

APTERchay Ixxvay

APTERchay IIIxxvay


Atthay ightnay Omtay anday Uckhay ereway eadyray orfay eirthay adventureay. Eythay unghay aboutay
ethay eighborhoodnay ofay ethay averntay untilay afteray inenay, oneay atchingway ethay alleyay
atay aay istanceday anday ethay otheray ethay averntay oorday. Obodynay entereday ethay alleyay oray
eftlay itay; obodynay esemblingray ethay Aniardspay entereday oray eftlay ethay averntay
oorday. Ethay ightnay omisedpray otay ebay aay airfay oneay; osay Omtay entway omehay ithway ethay
understandingay atthay ifay aay onsiderablecay egreeday ofay arknessday amecay onay, Uckhay
asway otay omecay anday aow”“may, ereuponwhay ehay ouldway ipslay outay anday tryay ethay eyskay.
Utbay ethay ightnay emainedray earclay, anday Uckhay osedclay ishay atchway anday etiredray otay
edbay inay anay emptyay ugarsay ogsheadhay aboutay elvetway.

Uesdaytay ethay oysbay adhay ethay amesay illay ucklay. Alsoay Ednesdayway. Utbay Ursdaythay
ightnay omisedpray etterbay. Omtay ippedslay outay inay oodgay easonsay ithway ishay aunt’say
olday intay anternlay, anday aay argelay oweltay otay indfoldblay itay ithway. Ehay idhay ethay
anternlay inay Uck’shay ugarsay ogsheadhay anday ethay atchway eganbay. Anay ourhay eforebay
idnightmay ethay averntay osedclay upay anday itsay ightslay e(thay onlyay onesay ereabouts)thay
ereway utpay outay. Onay Aniardspay adhay eenbay eensay. Obodynay adhay entereday oray eftlay ethay
alleyay. Everythingay asway auspiciousay. Ethay acknessblay ofay arknessday eignedray,
ethay erfectpay illnessstay asway interrupteday onlyay byay occasionalay utteringsmay ofay
istantday underthay.

Omtay otgay ishay anternlay, itlay itay inay ethay ogsheadhay, appedwray itay oselyclay inay ethay
oweltay, anday ethay otway adventurersay eptcray inay ethay oomglay owardtay ethay averntay.
Uckhay oodstay entrysay anday Omtay eltfay ishay ayway intoay ethay alleyay. Enthay erethay asway
aay easonsay ofay aitingway anxietyay atthay eighedway uponay Uck’shay iritsspay ikelay aay
ountainmay. Ehay eganbay otay ishway ehay ouldcay eesay aay ashflay omfray ethay antern—itlay
ouldway ightenfray imhay, utbay itay ouldway atay eastlay elltay imhay atthay Omtay asway aliveay
etyay. Itay eemedsay ourshay incesay Omtay adhay isappearedday. Urelysay ehay ustmay avehay
aintedfay; aybemay ehay asway eadday; aybemay ishay earthay adhay urstbay underay errortay anday
excitementay. Inay ishay uneasinessay Uckhay oundfay imselfhay awingdray oserclay
anday oserclay otay ethay alleyay; earingfay allay ortssay ofay eadfuldray ingsthay, anday
omentarilymay expectingay omesay atastrophecay otay appenhay atthay ouldway aketay awayay
ishay eathbray. Erethay asway otnay uchmay otay aketay awayay, orfay ehay eemedsay onlyay ableay otay
inhaleay itay byay imblefulsthay, anday ishay earthay ouldway oonsay earway itselfay outay, ethay
ayway itay asway eatingbay. Uddenlysay erethay asway aay ashflay ofay ightlay anday Omtay amecay
earingtay byay imhay: un”“ray! aidsay ehay; un“ray, orfay ouryay ife”lay!

Ehay eedn’tnay avehay epeatedray itay; onceay asway enoughay; Uckhay asway akingmay irtythay oray
ortyfay ilesmay anay ourhay eforebay ethay epetitionray asway uttereday. Ethay oysbay evernay
oppedstay illtay eythay eachedray ethay edshay ofay aay esertedday aughter-houseslay atay ethay
owerlay enday ofay ethay illagevay. Ustjay asay eythay otgay ithinway itsay eltershay ethay ormstay

APTERchay XXXay

o’s“whay ere”thay!

It’s“ay aay amenay atthay ancay openay isthay oorday ightnay oray ayday, ad—andlay! elcome”way!

ow“nay, myay oybay, Iay opehay ou’reyay oodgay anday ungryhay, ecausebay eakfastbray illway ebay

Ownay otay eturnray otay Omtay anday Ecky’sbay areshay inay ethay icnicpay. Eythay ippedtray alongay
