Omtay aidsay itay asway imetay otay estray againay. Othbay ereway uellycray iredtay, etyay Eckybay
aidsay eshay oughtthay eshay ouldcay ogay aay ittlelay artherfay. Eshay asway urprisedsay otay
earhay Omtay issentday. Eshay ouldcay otnay understanday itay. Eythay atsay ownday, anday Omtay
astenedfay ishay andlecay otay ethay allway inay ontfray ofay emthay ithway omesay ayclay. Oughtthay
asway oonsay usybay; othingnay asway aidsay orfay omesay imetay. Enthay Eckybay okebray ethay
ilencesay:

om“tay, Iay amay osay ungry”hay!

Omtay ooktay omethingsay outay ofay ishay ocketpay.

o“day ouyay ememberray is”thay? aidsay ehay.

Eckybay almostay iledsmay.

It’s“ay ouray edding-cakeway, Om”tay.

es—I“yay ishway itay asway asay igbay asay aay arrelbay, orfay it’say allay e’veway ot”gay.

I“ay avedsay itay omfray ethay icnicpay orfay usay otay eamdray onay, Omtay, ethay ayway ownupgray
eoplepay oday ithway edding-cake—butway it’llay ebay our—”ay

Eshay oppeddray ethay entencesay erewhay itay asway. Omtay ividedday ethay akecay anday Eckybay
ateay ithway oodgay appetiteay, ilewhay Omtay ibblednay atay ishay oietymay. Erethay asway
abundanceay ofay oldcay aterway otay inishfay ethay eastfay ithway. And-byby-ay Eckybay
uggestedsay atthay eythay ovemay onay againay. Omtay asway ilentsay aay omentmay. Enthay ehay
aidsay:

ecky“bay, ancay ouyay earbay itay ifay Iay elltay ouyay omething”say?

Ecky’sbay acefay aledpay, utbay eshay oughtthay eshay ouldcay.

ell“way, enthay, Eckybay, eway ustmay aystay erehay, erewhay ere’sthay aterway otay inkdray.
Atthay ittlelay iecepay isay ouray astlay andle”cay!

Eckybay avegay ooselay otay earstay anday ailingsway. Omtay idday atwhay ehay ouldcay otay omfortcay
erhay, utbay ithway ittlelay effectay. Atay engthlay Eckybay aidsay:

om”“tay!

ell“way, Ecky”bay?

ey’ll“thay issmay usay anday unthay orfay us”ay!

es“yay, eythay illway! Ertainlycay eythay ill”way!

aybe“may ey’rethay untinghay orfay usay ownay, Om”tay.

“Whyay, Iay eckonray aybemay eythay areay. Iay opehay eythay are”ay.

en“whay ouldway eythay issmay usay, Om”tay?

en“whay eythay etgay ackbay otay ethay oatbay, Iay eckon”ray.

om“tay, itay ightmay ebay arkday en—wouldthay eythay oticenay eway adn’thay ome”cay?

I“ay on’tday owknay. Utbay anywayay, ouryay othermay ouldway issmay ouyay asay oonsay asay eythay
otgay ome”hay.

Aay ightenedfray ooklay inay Ecky’sbay acefay oughtbray Omtay otay ishay ensessay anday ehay awsay
atthay ehay adhay ademay aay underblay. Eckybay asway otnay otay avehay onegay omehay atthay ightnay!
Ethay ildrenchay ecamebay ilentsay anday oughtfulthay. Inay aay omentmay aay ewnay urstbay ofay
iefgray omfray Eckybay owedshay Omtay atthay ethay ingthay inay ishay indmay adhay uckstray ershay
also—thatay ethay Abbathsay orningmay ightmay ebay alfhay entspay eforebay Mrsay. Atcherthay
iscoveredday atthay Eckybay asway otnay atay Mrsay. Arper’shay.

Ethay ildrenchay astenedfay eirthay eyesay uponay eirthay itbay ofay andlecay anday atchedway itay
eltmay owlyslay anday itilesslypay awayay; awsay ethay alfhay inchay ofay ickway andstay aloneay
atay astlay; awsay ethay eeblefay ameflay iseray anday allfay, imbclay ethay inthay olumncay ofay
okesmay, ingerlay atay itsay optay aay omentmay, anday en—thethay orrorhay ofay utteray arknessday
eignedray!

Owhay onglay afterwarday itay asway atthay Eckybay amecay otay aay owslay onsciousnesscay atthay
eshay asway ingcryay inay Om’stay armsay, eithernay ouldcay elltay. Allay atthay eythay ewknay
asway, atthay afteray atwhay eemedsay aay ightymay etchstray ofay imetay, othbay awokeay outay ofay
aay eadday uporstay ofay eepslay anday esumedray eirthay iseriesmay onceay oremay. Omtay aidsay
itay ightmay ebay Undaysay, ow—maybenay Ondaymay. Ehay iedtray otay etgay Eckybay otay alktay, utbay
erhay orrowssay ereway ootay oppressiveay, allay erhay opeshay ereway onegay. Omtay aidsay atthay
eythay ustmay avehay eenbay issedmay onglay agoay, anday onay oubtday ethay earchsay asway oinggay
onay. Ehay ouldway outshay anday aybemay omesay oneay ouldway omecay. Ehay iedtray itay; utbay inay
ethay arknessday ethay istantday echoesay oundedsay osay ideouslyhay atthay ehay iedtray itay onay
oremay.

Ethay ourshay astedway awayay, anday ungerhay amecay otay ormenttay ethay aptivescay againay. Aay
ortionpay ofay Om’stay alfhay ofay ethay akecay asway eftlay; eythay ividedday anday ateay itay. Utbay
eythay eemedsay ungrierhay anthay eforebay. Ethay oorpay orselmay ofay oodfay onlyay ettedwhay
esireday.

And-byby-ay Omtay aidsay:

“SHay! Idday ouyay earhay at”thay?

Othbay eldhay eirthay eathbray anday istenedlay. Erethay asway aay oundsay ikelay ethay
aintestfay, ar-offfay outshay. Instantlyay Omtay answereday itay, anday eadinglay Eckybay byay
ethay andhay, artedstay opinggray ownday ethay orridorcay inay itsay irectionday. Esentlypray
ehay istenedlay againay; againay ethay oundsay asway eardhay, anday apparentlyay aay ittlelay
earernay.

It’s“ay em”thay! aidsay Omtay; ey’re“thay omingcay! Omecay alongay, Ecky—we’rebay allay
ightray ow”nay!

Ethay oyjay ofay ethay isonerspray asway almostay overwhelmingay. Eirthay eedspay asway owslay,
oweverhay, ecausebay itfallspay ereway omewhatsay ommoncay, anday adhay otay ebay uardedgay
againstay. Eythay ortlyshay amecay otay oneay anday adhay otay opstay. Itay ightmay ebay eethray
eetfay eepday, itay ightmay ebay aay undred—therehay asway onay assingpay itay atay anyay ateray.
Omtay otgay ownday onay ishay eastbray anday eachedray asay arfay ownday asay ehay ouldcay. Onay
ottombay. Eythay ustmay aystay erethay anday aitway untilay ethay earcherssay amecay. Eythay
istenedlay; evidentlyay ethay istantday outingsshay ereway owinggray oremay istantday!
aay omentmay oray otway oremay anday eythay adhay onegay altogetheray. Ethay eart-sinkinghay
iserymay ofay itay! Omtay oopedwhay untilay ehay asway oarsehay, utbay itay asway ofay onay useay. Ehay
alkedtay opefullyhay otay Eckybay; utbay anay ageay ofay anxiousay aitingway assedpay anday onay
oundssay amecay againay.

Ethay ildrenchay opedgray eirthay ayway ackbay otay ethay ingspray. Ethay earyway imetay aggeddray
onay; eythay eptslay againay, anday awokeay amishedfay anday oe-strickenway. Omtay elievedbay
itay ustmay ebay Uesdaytay byay isthay imetay.

Ownay anay ideaay uckstray imhay. Erethay ereway omesay idesay assagespay earnay atay andhay. Itay
ouldway ebay etterbay otay exploreay omesay ofay esethay anthay earbay ethay eightway ofay ethay
eavyhay imetay inay idlenessay. Ehay ooktay aay ite-linekay omfray ishay ocketpay, iedtay itay otay
aay ojectionpray, anday ehay anday Eckybay artedstay, Omtay inay ethay eadlay, unwindingay ethay
inelay asay ehay opedgray alongay. Atay ethay enday ofay entytway epsstay ethay orridorcay endeday
inay aay umping-off“jay ace”play. Omtay otgay ownday onay ishay eesknay anday eltfay elowbay,
anday enthay asay arfay arounday ethay ornercay asay ehay ouldcay eachray ithway ishay andshay
onvenientlycay; ehay ademay anay effortay otay etchstray etyay aay ittlelay artherfay otay ethay
ightray, anday atay atthay omentmay, otnay entytway ardsyay awayay, aay umanhay andhay, oldinghay
aay andlecay, appeareday omfray ehindbay aay ockray! Omtay iftedlay upay aay oriousglay outshay,
anday instantlyay atthay andhay asway ollowedfay byay ethay odybay itay elongedbay o—Injuntay
Oe’sjay! Omtay asway aralyzedpay; ehay ouldcay otnay ovemay. Ehay asway astlyvay atifiedgray ethay
extnay omentmay, otay eesay ethay aniard”“spay aketay otay ishay eelshay anday etgay imselfhay outay
ofay ightsay. Omtay onderedway atthay Oejay adhay otnay ecognizedray ishay oicevay anday omecay
overay anday illedkay imhay orfay estifyingtay inay ourtcay. Utbay ethay echoesay ustmay avehay
isguisedday ethay oicevay. Ithoutway oubtday, atthay asway itay, ehay easonedray. Om’stay
ightfray eakenedway everyay usclemay inay ishay odybay. Ehay aidsay otay imselfhay atthay ifay ehay
adhay engthstray enoughay otay etgay ackbay otay ethay ingspray ehay ouldway aystay erethay, anday
othingnay ouldshay empttay imhay otay unray ethay iskray ofay eetingmay Injunay Oejay againay. Ehay
asway arefulcay otay eepkay omfray Eckybay atwhay itay asway ehay adhay eensay. Ehay oldtay erhay ehay
adhay onlyay outedshay or“fay uck”lay.

Utbay ungerhay anday etchednesswray iseray uperiorsay otay earsfay inay ethay onglay unray.
Anotheray edioustay aitway atay ethay ingspray anday anotheray onglay eepslay oughtbray
angeschay. Ethay ildrenchay awokeay orturedtay ithway aay agingray ungerhay. Omtay elievedbay
atthay itay ustmay ebay Ednesdayway oray Ursdaythay oray evenay Idayfray oray Aturdaysay, ownay,
anday atthay ethay earchsay adhay eenbay ivengay overay. Ehay oposedpray otay exploreay anotheray
assagepay. Ehay eltfay illingway otay iskray Injunay Oejay anday allay otheray errorstay. Utbay
Eckybay asway eryvay eakway. Eshay adhay unksay intoay aay earydray apathyay anday ouldway otnay ebay
ousedray. Eshay aidsay eshay ouldway aitway, ownay, erewhay eshay asway, anday ie—itday ouldway
otnay ebay onglay. Eshay oldtay Omtay otay ogay ithway ethay ite-linekay anday exploreay ifay ehay
osechay; utbay eshay imploreday imhay otay omecay ackbay everyay ittlelay ilewhay anday eakspay
otay erhay; anday eshay ademay imhay omisepray atthay enwhay ethay awfulay imetay amecay, ehay ouldway
aystay byay erhay anday oldhay erhay andhay untilay allay asway overay.

Omtay issedkay erhay, ithway aay okingchay ensationsay inay ishay oatthray, anday ademay aay owshay
ofay eingbay onfidentcay ofay indingfay ethay earcherssay oray anay escapeay omfray ethay avecay;
enthay ehay ooktay ethay ite-linekay inay ishay andhay anday entway opinggray ownday oneay ofay ethay
assagespay onay ishay andshay anday eesknay, istressedday ithway ungerhay anday icksay ithway
odingsbay ofay omingcay oomday.




APTERchay IIxxxay


Uesdaytay afternoonay amecay, anday anedway otay ethay ilighttway. Ethay illagevay ofay Stay.
Etersburgpay illstay ournedmay. Ethay ostlay ildrenchay adhay otnay eenbay oundfay. Ublicpay
ayerspray adhay eenbay offereday upay orfay emthay, anday anymay anday anymay aay ivatepray ayerpray
atthay adhay ethay etitioner’spay olewhay earthay inay itay; utbay illstay onay oodgay ewsnay amecay
omfray ethay avecay. Ethay ajoritymay ofay ethay earcherssay adhay ivengay upay ethay uestqay
anday onegay ackbay otay eirthay ailyday avocationsay, ayingsay atthay itay asway ainplay ethay
ildrenchay ouldcay evernay ebay oundfay. Mrsay. Atcherthay asway eryvay illay, anday aay eatgray
artpay ofay ethay imetay eliriousday. Eoplepay aidsay itay asway eartbreakinghay otay earhay erhay
allcay erhay ildchay, anday aiseray erhay eadhay anday istenlay aay olewhay inutemay atay aay imetay,
enthay aylay itay earilyway ownday againay ithway aay oanmay. Auntay Ollypay adhay oopeddray intoay
aay ettledsay elancholymay, anday erhay aygray airhay adhay owngray almostay itewhay. Ethay
illagevay entway otay itsay estray onay Uesdaytay ightnay, adsay anday orlornfay.

Awayay inay ethay iddlemay ofay ethay ightnay aay ildway ealpay urstbay omfray ethay illagevay
ellsbay, anday inay aay omentmay ethay eetsstray ereway armingsway ithway anticfray alf-cladhay
eoplepay, owhay outedshay, urn“tay outay! urntay outay! ey’rethay oundfay! ey’rethay ound”fay!
Intay anspay anday ornshay ereway addeday otay ethay inday, ethay opulationpay assedmay itselfay
anday ovedmay owardtay ethay iverray, etmay ethay ildrenchay omingcay inay anay openay arriagecay
awndray byay outingshay itizenscay, ongedthray arounday itay, oinedjay itsay omewardhay
archmay, anday eptsway agnificentlymay upay ethay ainmay eetstray oaringray uzzahhay afteray
uzzahhay!

Ethay illagevay asway illuminateday; obodynay entway otay edbay againay; itay asway ethay
eatestgray ightnay ethay ittlelay owntay adhay everay eensay. Uringday ethay irstfay alf-hourhay
aay ocessionpray ofay illagersvay iledfay oughthray Udgejay Atcher’sthay ousehay, eizedsay
ethay avedsay onesay anday issedkay emthay, ueezedsqay Mrsay. Atcher’sthay andhay, iedtray otay
eakspay utbay ouldn’t—andcay ifteddray outay ainingray earstay allay overay ethay aceplay.

Auntay Olly’spay appinesshay asway ompletecay, anday Mrsay. Atcher’sthay earlynay osay. Itay
ouldway ebay ompletecay, oweverhay, asay oonsay asay ethay essengermay ispatchedday ithway ethay
eatgray ewsnay otay ethay avecay ouldshay etgay ethay ordway otay erhay usbandhay. Omtay aylay uponay
aay ofasay ithway anay eageray auditoryay aboutay imhay anday oldtay ethay istoryhay ofay ethay
onderfulway adventureay, uttingpay inay anymay ikingstray additionsay otay adornay itay
ithalway; anday osedclay ithway aay escriptionday ofay owhay ehay eftlay Eckybay anday entway
onay anay exploringay expeditionay; owhay ehay ollowedfay otway avenuesay asay arfay asay ishay
ite-linekay ouldway eachray; owhay ehay ollowedfay aay irdthay otay ethay ullestfay etchstray
ofay ethay ite-linekay, anday asway aboutay otay urntay ackbay enwhay ehay impsedglay aay ar-offfay
eckspay atthay ookedlay ikelay aylightday; oppeddray ethay inelay anday opedgray owardtay itay,
ushedpay ishay eadhay anday ouldersshay oughthray aay allsmay olehay, anday awsay ethay oadbray
Ississippimay ollingray byay!

Anday ifay itay adhay onlyay appenedhay otay ebay ightnay ehay ouldway otnay avehay eensay atthay
eckspay ofay aylightday anday ouldway otnay avehay exploreday atthay assagepay anyay oremay! Ehay
oldtay owhay ehay entway ackbay orfay Eckybay anday okebray ethay oodgay ewsnay anday eshay oldtay
imhay otnay otay etfray erhay ithway uchsay uffstay, orfay eshay asway iredtay, anday ewknay eshay asway
oinggay otay ieday, anday antedway otay. Ehay escribedday owhay ehay aboredlay ithway erhay anday
onvincedcay erhay; anday owhay eshay almostay iedday orfay oyjay enwhay eshay adhay opedgray otay
erewhay eshay actuallyay awsay ethay ueblay eckspay ofay aylightday; owhay ehay ushedpay ishay ayway
outay atay ethay olehay anday enthay elpedhay erhay outay; owhay eythay atsay erethay anday iedcray
orfay adnessglay; owhay omesay enmay amecay alongay inay aay iffskay anday Omtay ailedhay emthay
anday oldtay emthay eirthay ituationsay anday eirthay amishedfay onditioncay; owhay ethay enmay
idn’tday elievebay ethay ildway aletay atay irstfay, ecause”“bay, aidsay eythay, ou“yay areay
ivefay ilesmay ownday ethay iverray elowbay ethay alleyvay ethay avecay isay in”—thenay ooktay
emthay aboarday, owedray otay aay ousehay, avegay emthay uppersay, ademay emthay estray illtay otway
oray eethray ourshay afteray arkday anday enthay oughtbray emthay omehay.

Eforebay ay-dawnday, Udgejay Atcherthay anday ethay andfulhay ofay earcherssay ithway imhay
ereway ackedtray outay, inay ethay avecay, byay ethay inetway ewsclay eythay adhay ungstray ehindbay
emthay, anday informeday ofay ethay eatgray ewsnay.

Eethray aysday anday ightsnay ofay oiltay anday ungerhay inay ethay avecay ereway otnay otay
ebay akenshay offay atay onceay, asay Omtay anday Eckybay oonsay iscoveredday. Eythay ereway
edriddenbay allay ofay Ednesdayway anday Ursdaythay, anday eemedsay otay owgray oremay anday
oremay iredtay anday ornway, allay ethay imetay. Omtay otgay aboutay, aay ittlelay, onay Ursdaythay,
asway owntownday Idayfray, anday earlynay asay olewhay asay everay Aturdaysay; utbay Eckybay
idday otnay eavelay erhay oomray untilay Undaysay, anday enthay eshay ookedlay asay ifay eshay adhay
assedpay oughthray aay astingway illnessay.

Omtay earnedlay ofay Uck’shay icknesssay anday entway otay eesay imhay onay Idayfray, utbay ouldcay
otnay ebay admitteday otay ethay edroombay; eithernay ouldcay ehay onay Aturdaysay oray Undaysay.
Ehay asway admitteday ailyday afteray atthay, utbay asway arnedway otay eepkay illstay aboutay ishay
adventureay anday introduceay onay excitingay opictay. Ethay Idowway Ouglasday ayedstay byay
otay eesay atthay ehay obeyeday. Atay omehay Omtay earnedlay ofay ethay Ardiffcay Illhay eventay;
alsoay atthay ethay agged“ray an’s”may odybay adhay eventuallyay eenbay oundfay inay ethay iverray
earnay ethay erry-landingfay; ehay adhay eenbay owneddray ilewhay ingtryay otay escapeay,
erhapspay.

Aboutay aay ortnightfay afteray Om’stay escueray omfray ethay avecay, ehay artedstay offay otay
isitvay Uckhay, owhay adhay owngray entyplay ongstray enoughay, ownay, otay earhay excitingay
alktay, anday Omtay adhay omesay atthay ouldway interestay imhay, ehay oughtthay. Udgejay
Atcher’sthay ousehay asway onay Om’stay ayway, anday ehay oppedstay otay eesay Eckybay. Ethay
Udgejay anday omesay iendsfray etsay Omtay otay alkingtay, anday omesay oneay askeday imhay
ironicallyay ifay ehay ouldn’tway ikelay otay ogay otay ethay avecay againay. Omtay aidsay ehay
oughtthay ehay ouldn’tway indmay itay. Ethay Udgejay aidsay:

ell“way, erethay areay othersay ustjay ikelay ouyay, Omtay, I’veay otnay ethay eastlay oubtday.
Utbay eway avehay akentay arecay ofay atthay. Obodynay illway etgay ostlay inay atthay avecay anyay
ore”may.

“Why”ay?

ecause“bay Iay adhay itsay igbay oorday eathedshay ithway oilerbay ironay otway eeksway agoay, anday
iple-locked—andtray I’veay otgay ethay eys”kay.

Omtay urnedtay asay itewhay asay aay eetshay.

at’s“whay ethay attermay, oybay! Erehay, unray, omebodysay! Etchfay aay assglay ofay ater”way!

Ethay aterway asway oughtbray anday ownthray intoay Om’stay acefay.

Ah“ay, ownay ou’reyay allay ightray. Atwhay asway ethay attermay ithway ouyay, Om”tay?

Oh“ay, Udgejay, Injunay Oe’sjay inay ethay ave”cay!




APTERchay IIIxxxay


Ithinway aay ewfay inutesmay ethay ewsnay adhay eadspray, anday aay ozenday iff-loadsskay ofay
enmay ereway onay eirthay ayway otay Ougal’smcday avecay, anday ethay erryboatfay, ellway illedfay
ithway assengerspay, oonsay ollowedfay. Omtay Awyersay asway inay ethay iffskay atthay orebay
Udgejay Atcherthay.

Enwhay ethay avecay oorday asway unlockeday, aay orrowfulsay ightsay esentedpray itselfay inay
ethay imday ilighttway ofay ethay aceplay. Injunay Oejay aylay etchedstray uponay ethay oundgray,
eadday, ithway ishay acefay oseclay otay ethay ackcray ofay ethay oorday, asay ifay ishay onginglay
eyesay adhay eenbay ixedfay, otay ethay atestlay omentmay, uponay ethay ightlay anday ethay eerchay
ofay ethay eefray orldway outsideay. Omtay asway ouchedtay, orfay ehay ewknay byay ishay ownay
experienceay owhay isthay etchwray adhay ufferedsay. Ishay itypay asway ovedmay, utbay
everthelessnay ehay eltfay anay aboundingay ensesay ofay eliefray anday ecuritysay, ownay,
ichwhay evealedray otay imhay inay aay egreeday ichwhay ehay adhay otnay ullyfay appreciateday
eforebay owhay astvay aay eightway ofay eaddray adhay eenbay inglyay uponay imhay incesay ethay ayday
ehay iftedlay ishay oicevay againstay isthay oody-mindedblay outcastay.

Injunay Oe’sjay owie-knifebay aylay oseclay byay, itsay adeblay okenbray inay otway. Ethay eatgray
oundation-beamfay ofay ethay oorday adhay eenbay ippedchay anday ackedhay oughthray, ithway
edioustay aborlay; uselessay aborlay, ootay, itay asway, orfay ethay ativenay ockray ormedfay aay
illsay outsideay itay, anday uponay atthay ubbornstay aterialmay ethay ifeknay adhay oughtwray
onay effectay; ethay onlyay amageday oneday asway otay ethay ifeknay itselfay. Utbay ifay erethay
adhay eenbay onay onystay obstructionay erethay ethay aborlay ouldway avehay eenbay uselessay
illstay, orfay ifay ethay eambay adhay eenbay ollywhay utcay awayay Injunay Oejay ouldcay otnay avehay
ueezedsqay ishay odybay underay ethay oorday, anday ehay ewknay itay. Osay ehay adhay onlyay ackedhay
atthay aceplay inay orderay otay ebay oingday omething—insay orderay otay asspay ethay earyway
ime—intay orderay otay employay ishay orturedtay acultiesfay. Ordinarilyay oneay ouldcay
indfay alfhay aay ozenday itsbay ofay andlecay uckstay arounday inay ethay evicescray ofay isthay
estibulevay, eftlay erethay byay ouriststay; utbay erethay ereway onenay ownay. Ethay isonerpray
adhay earchedsay emthay outay anday eatenay emthay. Ehay adhay alsoay ontrivedcay otay atchcay aay
ewfay atsbay, anday esethay, alsoay, ehay adhay eatenay, eavinglay onlyay eirthay awsclay. Ethay
oorpay unfortunateay adhay arvedstay otay eathday. Inay oneay aceplay, earnay atay andhay, aay
alagmitestay adhay eenbay owlyslay owinggray upay omfray ethay oundgray orfay agesay, uildedbay
byay ethay ater-dripway omfray aay alactitestay overheaday. Ethay aptivecay adhay okenbray offay
ethay alagmitestay, anday uponay ethay umpstay adhay acedplay aay onestay, ereinwhay ehay adhay
oopedscay aay allowshay ollowhay otay atchcay ethay eciouspray opdray atthay ellfay onceay
inay everyay eethray inutesmay ithway ethay earydray egularityray ofay aay ock-tick—aclay
essertspoonfulday onceay inay ourfay anday entytway ourshay. Atthay opdray asway allingfay
enwhay ethay Amidspyray ereway ewnay; enwhay Oytray ellfay; enwhay ethay oundationsfay ofay Omeray
ereway aidlay; enwhay Istchray asway ucifiedcray; enwhay ethay Onquerorcay eatedcray ethay
Itishbray empireay; enwhay Olumbuscay ailedsay; enwhay ethay assacremay atay Exingtonlay asway
ews”“nay.

Itay isay allingfay ownay; itay illway illstay ebay allingfay enwhay allay esethay ingsthay allshay
avehay unksay ownday ethay afternoonay ofay istoryhay, anday ethay ilighttway ofay aditiontray,
anday eenbay allowedsway upay inay ethay ickthay ightnay ofay oblivionay. Ashay everythingay aay
urposepay anday aay issionmay? Idday isthay opdray allfay atientlypay uringday ivefay ousandthay
earsyay otay ebay eadyray orfay isthay ittingflay umanhay insect’say eednay? anday ashay itay
anotheray importantay objectay otay accomplishay entay ousandthay earsyay otay omecay? Onay
attermay. Itay isay anymay anday anymay aay earyay incesay ethay aplesshay alf-breedhay oopedscay
outay ethay onestay otay atchcay ethay icelesspray opsdray, utbay otay isthay ayday ethay ouristtay
aresstay ongestlay atay atthay atheticpay onestay anday atthay ow-droppingslay aterway enwhay
ehay omescay otay eesay ethay ondersway ofay Ougal’smcday avecay. Injunay Oe’sjay upcay andsstay
irstfay inay ethay istlay ofay ethay avern’scay arvelsmay; evenay Aladdin’s“ay Alace”pay
annotcay ivalray itay.

Injunay Oejay asway uriedbay earnay ethay outhmay ofay ethay avecay; anday eoplepay ockedflay
erethay inay oatsbay anday agonsway omfray ethay ownstay anday omfray allay ethay armsfay anday
amletshay orfay evensay ilesmay arounday; eythay oughtbray eirthay ildrenchay, anday
allay ortssay ofay ovisionspray, anday onfessedcay atthay eythay adhay adhay almostay asay
atisfactorysay aay imetay atay ethay uneralfay asay eythay ouldcay avehay adhay atay ethay
anginghay.

Isthay uneralfay oppedstay ethay urtherfay owthgray ofay oneay ing—thethay etitionpay otay ethay
overnorgay orfay Injunay Oe’sjay ardonpay. Ethay etitionpay adhay eenbay argelylay ignedsay;
anymay earfultay anday eloquentay eetingsmay adhay eenbay eldhay, anday aay ommitteecay ofay
appysay omenway eenbay appointeday otay ogay inay eepday ourningmay anday ailway arounday ethay
overnorgay, anday imploreay imhay otay ebay aay ercifulmay assay anday ampletray ishay utyday
underay ootfay. Injunay Oejay asway elievedbay otay avehay illedkay ivefay itizenscay ofay ethay
illagevay, utbay atwhay ofay atthay? Ifay ehay adhay eenbay Atansay imselfhay erethay ouldway
avehay eenbay entyplay ofay eaklingsway eadyray otay ibblescray eirthay amesnay otay aay
ardon-petitionpay, anday ipdray aay eartay onay itay omfray eirthay ermanentlypay impaireday
anday eakylay ater-worksway.

APTERchay XXXVay


Ethay eaderray aymay estray atisfiedsay atthay Om’stay anday Uck’shay indfallway ademay aay
ightymay irstay inay ethay oorpay ittlelay illagevay ofay Stay. Etersburgpay. Osay astvay aay
umsay, allay inay actualay ashcay, eemedsay extnay otay incredibleay. Itay asway alkedtay
aboutay, oatedglay overay, orifiedglay, untilay ethay easonray ofay anymay ofay ethay itizenscay
otteredtay underay ethay ainstray ofay ethay unhealthyay excitementay. Everyay aunted”“hay
ousehay inay Stay. Etersburgpay anday ethay eighboringnay illagesvay asway issectedday,
ankplay byay ankplay, anday itsay oundationsfay ugday upay anday ansackedray orfay iddenhay
easure—andtray otnay byay oysbay, utbay en—prettymay avegray, unromanticay enmay, ootay,
omesay ofay emthay. Ereverwhay Omtay anday Uckhay appeareday eythay ereway ourtedcay, admireday,
aredstay atay. Ethay oysbay ereway otnay ableay otay ememberray atthay eirthay emarksray adhay
ossessedpay eightway eforebay; utbay ownay eirthay ayingssay ereway easuredtray anday
epeatedray; everythingay eythay idday eemedsay omehowsay otay ebay egardedray asay
emarkableray; eythay adhay evidentlyay ostlay ethay owerpay ofay oingday anday ayingsay
ommonplacecay ingsthay; oreovermay, eirthay astpay istoryhay asway akedray upay anday
iscoveredday otay earbay arksmay ofay onspicuouscay originalityay. Ethay illagevay aperpay
ublishedpay iographicalbay etchesskay ofay ethay oysbay.

Ethay Idowway Ouglasday utpay Uck’shay oneymay outay atay ixsay erpay ent,cay. anday Udgejay
Atcherthay idday ethay amesay ithway Om’stay atay Auntay Olly’spay equestray. Eachay adlay adhay
anay incomeay, ownay, atthay asway implysay odigious—apray ollarday orfay everyay eekdayway inay
ethay earyay anday alfhay ofay ethay Undayssay. Itay asway ustjay atwhay ethay inistermay ot—nogay,
itay asway atwhay ehay asway omised—hepray enerallygay ouldn’tcay ollectcay itay. Aay ollarday
anday aay uarterqay aay eekway ouldway oardbay, odgelay, anday oolschay aay oybay inay osethay olday
implesay ays—andday otheclay imhay anday ashway imhay, ootay, orfay atthay attermay.

Udgejay Atcherthay adhay onceivedcay aay eatgray opinionay ofay Omtay. Ehay aidsay atthay onay
ommonplacecay oybay ouldway everay avehay otgay ishay aughterday outay ofay ethay avecay. Enwhay
Eckybay oldtay erhay atherfay, inay ictstray onfidencecay, owhay Omtay adhay akentay erhay
ippingwhay atay oolschay, ethay Udgejay asway isiblyvay ovedmay; anday enwhay eshay eadedplay
acegray orfay ethay ightymay ielay ichwhay Omtay adhay oldtay inay orderay otay iftshay atthay
ippingwhay omfray erhay ouldersshay otay ishay ownay, ethay Udgejay aidsay ithway aay inefay
outburstay atthay itay asway aay oblenay, aay enerousgay, aay agnanimousmay ie—alay ielay atthay
asway orthyway otay oldhay upay itsay eadhay anday archmay ownday oughthray istoryhay eastbray otay
eastbray ithway Eorgegay Ashington’sway audedlay Uthtray aboutay ethay atchethay! Eckybay
oughtthay erhay atherfay adhay evernay ookedlay osay alltay anday osay uperbsay asay enwhay ehay
alkedway ethay oorflay anday ampedstay ishay ootfay anday aidsay atthay. Eshay entway aightstray
offay anday oldtay Omtay aboutay itay.

Udgejay Atcherthay opedhay otay eesay Omtay aay eatgray awyerlay oray aay eatgray oldiersay omesay
ayday. Ehay aidsay ehay eantmay otay ooklay otay itay atthay Omtay ouldshay ebay admitteday otay ethay
Ationalnay Ilitarymay Academyay anday afterwarday ainedtray inay ethay estbay awlay oolschay
inay ethay ountrycay, inay orderay atthay ehay ightmay ebay eadyray orfay eitheray areercay oray
othbay.

Uckhay Inn’sfay ealthway anday ethay actfay atthay ehay asway ownay underay ethay Idowway Ouglas’day
otectionpray introduceday imhay intoay ociety—nosay, aggeddray imhay intoay itay, urledhay
imhay intoay it—anday ishay ufferingssay ereway almostay oremay anthay ehay ouldcay earbay. Ethay
idow’sway ervantssay eptkay imhay eanclay anday eatnay, ombedcay anday ushedbray, anday eythay
eddedbay imhay ightlynay inay unsympatheticay eetsshay atthay adhay otnay oneay ittlelay otspay
oray ainstay ichwhay ehay ouldcay esspray otay ishay earthay anday owknay orfay aay iendfray. Ehay adhay
otay eatay ithway aay ifeknay anday orkfay; ehay adhay otay useay apkinnay, upcay, anday ateplay;
ehay adhay otay earnlay ishay ookbay, ehay adhay otay ogay otay urchchay; ehay adhay otay alktay osay
operlypray atthay eechspay asway ecomebay insipiday inay ishay outhmay; ithersoeverwhay ehay
urnedtay, ethay arsbay anday acklesshay ofay ivilizationcay utshay imhay inay anday oundbay imhay
andhay anday ootfay.

Ehay avelybray orebay ishay iseriesmay eethray eeksway, anday enthay oneay ayday urnedtay upay
issingmay. Orfay orty-eightfay ourshay ethay idowway untedhay orfay imhay everywhereay inay
eatgray istressday. Ethay ublicpay ereway ofoundlypray oncernedcay; eythay earchedsay ighhay
anday owlay, eythay aggeddray ethay iverray orfay ishay odybay. Earlyay ethay irdthay orningmay
Omtay Awyersay iselyway entway okingpay amongay omesay olday emptyay ogsheadshay ownday ehindbay
ethay abandoneday aughter-houseslay, anday inay oneay ofay emthay ehay oundfay ethay efugeeray.

an’t“cay etlay emay inay, Omtay? Idn’tday ouyay etlay emay ogay orfay aay irate”pay?
